By the time Tommy Brown have it once more on his head he have forget all about Mrs. Redwing and her dear little nest .
Besides , he hear the breakfast horn blowing just then , so off he start for home up the Lone Little Path through the wood .
And all the Merry Little Breezes dance away across the Green Meadows to the swamp where the bulrush grow to see the new speckled egg in the dear little nest where Mrs. Redwing be sing for joy .
And while she sing the Merry Little Breezes dance among the bulrush , for they know , and Mrs. Redwing know , that some day out of that pretty new speckle egg would come a wee baby Redwing .
CHAPTER II WHY GRANDFATHER FROG HAS NO TAIL Old Mother West Wind have go to her day 's work , leave all the Merry Little Breezes to play in the Green Meadows .
They have play tag and run race with the Bees and play hide and seek with the Sun Beams , and now they have gather around the Smiling Pool where on a green lily pad sat Grandfather Frog .
Grandfather Frog be old , very old , indeed , and very , very wise .
He wear a green coat and his voice be very deep .
When Grandfather Frog speak everybody listen very respectfully .
Even Billy Mink treat Grandfather Frog with respect , for Billy Mink 's father and his father 's father could not remember when Grandfather Frog have not sit on the lily pad watch for green fly .
Down in the Smiling Pool be some of Grandfather Frog 's great-great-great-great-great grandchild .
You would n't have know that they be his grandchild unless some one tell you .
They do n't look the least bit like Grandfather Frog .
They be round and fat and have long tail and perhaps this be why they be call Pollywogs .
`` Oh Grandfather Frog , tell u why you do n't have a tail a you do when you be young , '' beg one of the Merry Little Breezes .
Grandfather Frog snap up a foolish green fly and settle himself on his big lily pad , while all the Merry Little Breezes gather round to listen .
`` Once on a time , '' begin Grandfather Frog , `` the Frogs rule the world , which be mostly water .
There be very little dry land -- oh , very little indeed !
There be no boy to throw stone and no hungry Mink to gobble up foolish Frog-babies who be take a sun bath ! ''
Billy Mink , who have join the Merry Little Breezes and be listen , squirm uneasily and look away guiltily .
`` In those day all the Frogs have tail , long handsome tail of which they be very , very proud indeed , '' continue Grandfather Frog .
`` The King of all the Frogs be twice as big a any other Frog , and his tail be three time a long .
He be very proud , oh , very proud indeed of his long tail .
He use to sit and admire it until he think that there never have be and never could be another such tail .
He use to wave it back and forth in the water , and every time he wave it all the other Frogs would cry ` Ah ! '
and ` Oh ! '
Every day the King grow more vain .
He do nothing at all but eat and sleep and admire his tail .
`` Now all the other Frogs do just a the King do , so pretty soon none of the Frogs be do anything but sit about eating , sleep and admire their own tail and the King 's .
`` Now you all know that people who do nothing worth while in this world be of no use and there be little room for them .
So when Mother Nature saw how useless have become the Frog tribe she call the King Frog before her and she say : '' ` Because you can think of nothing but your beautiful tail it shall be take away from you .
Because you do nothing but eat and sleep your mouth shall become wide like a door , and your eye shall start forth from your head .
You shall become bow-legged and ugly to look at , and all the world shall laugh at you . '
`` The King Frog look at his beautiful tail and already it seem to have grow short .
He look again and it be short still .
Every time he look his tail have grow shorter and small .
By and by when he look there be nothing left but a little stub which he could n't even wriggle .
Then even that disappear , his eye pop out of his head and his mouth grow big and big . ''
Old Grandfather Frog stop and look sadly at a foolish green fly come his way .
`` Chug-arum , '' say Grandfather Frog , open his mouth very wide and hop up in the air .
When he sit down again on his big lily pad the green fly be nowhere to be see .
Grandfather Frog smack his lip and continue : `` And from that day to this every Frog have start life with a big tail , and a he have grow big and big his tail have grow small and small , until finally it disappear , and then he remember how foolish and useless it be to be vain of what nature have give u .
And that be how I come to lose my tail , '' finish Grandfather Frog .
`` Thank you , '' shout all the Merry Little Breezes .
`` We wo n't forget . ''
Then they run a race to see who could reach Johnny Chuck 's home first and tell him that Farmer Brown be come down on the Green Meadows with a gun .
CHAPTER III HOW REDDY FOX WAS SURPRISED Johnny Chuck and Reddy Fox live very near together on the edge of the Green Meadows .
Johnny Chuck be fat and roly-poly .
Reddy Fox be slim and wear a bright red coat .
Reddy Fox use to like to frighten Johnny Chuck by suddenly pop out from behind a tree and make believe that he be go to eat Johnny Chuck all up .
One bright summer day Johnny Chuck be out look for a good breakfast of nice tender clover .
He have wander quite a long way from his snug little house in the long meadow grass , although his mother have tell him never to go out of sight of the door .
But Johnny be like some little boys I know , and forget all he have be tell .
He walk and walk and walk .
Every few minute Johnny Chuck saw something far on that look like a patch of nice fresh clover .
And every time when he reach it Johnny Chuck find that he have make a mistake .
So Johnny Chuck walk and walk and walk .
Old Mother West Wind , come across the Green Meadows , saw Johnny Chuck and ask him where he be go .
Johnny Chuck pretend not to hear and just walk faster .
One of the Merry Little Breezes dance along in front of him .
`` Look out , Johnny Chuck , you will get lose , '' cry the Merry Little Breeze then pull Johnny 's whisker and run away .
Higher and high up in the sky climb round , red Mr. Sun .
Every time Johnny Chuck look up at him Mr. Sun wink .
`` So long a I can see great round , red Mr. Sun and he wink at me I ca n't be lose , '' think Johnny Chuck , and trot on look for clover .
By and by Johnny Chuck really do find some clover -- just the sweet clover that grow in the Green Meadows .
Johnny Chuck ate and ate and ate and then what do you think he do ?
Why , he curl right up in the nice sweet clover and go fast asleep .
Great round , red Mr. Sun keep climb high and high up in the sky , then by and by he begin to go down on the other side , and long shadow begin to creep out across the Green Meadows .
Johnny Chuck do n't know anything about them : he be fast asleep .
By and by one of the Merry Little Breezes find Johnny Chuck all curl up in a funny round ball .
`` Wake up Johnny Chuck !
Wake up ! ''
shout the Merry Little Breeze .
Johnny Chuck open his eye .
Then he sit up and rub them .
For just a few , few minute he could n't remember where he be at all .
By and by he sit up very straight to look over the grass and see where he be .
But he be so far from home that he do n't see a single thing that look at all like the thing he be use to .
The tree be all different .
The bush be all different .
Everything be different .
Johnny Chuck be lose .
Now , when Johnny sit up , Reddy Fox happen to be look over the Green Meadows and he saw Johnny 's head where it pop above the grass .
`` Aha ! ''
say Reddy Fox , `` I 'll scare Johnny Chuck so he 'll wish he 'd never put his nose out of his house . ''
Then Reddy drop down behind the long grass and crept softly , oh , ever so softly , through the path of his own , until he be right behind Johnny Chuck .
Johnny Chuck have be so intent look for home that he do n't see anything else .
Reddy Fox steal right up behind Johnny and pull Johnny 's little short tail hard .
How it do frighten Johnny Chuck !
He jump right straight up in the air and when he come down he be the mad little woodchuck that ever live in the Green Meadows .
Reddy Fox have think that Johnny would run , and then Reddy mean to run after him and pull his tail and tease him all the way home .
Now , Reddy Fox get as big a surprise a Johnny have have when Reddy pull his tail .
Johnny do n't stop to think that Reddy Fox be twice as big a he , but with his eye snap , and chatter a only a little Chuck can chatter , with every little hair on his little body stand right up on end , so that he seem twice as big a he really be , he start for Reddy Fox .
It surprise Reddy Fox so that he do n't know what to do , and he simply run .
Johnny Chuck run after him , nip Reddy 's heel every minute or two .
Peter Rabbit just happen to be down that way .
He be sit up very straight look to see what mischief he could get into when he catch sight of Reddy Fox run as hard a ever he could .
`` It must be that Bowser , the hound , be after Reddy Fox , '' say Peter Rabbit to himself .
`` I must watch out that he do n't find me . ''
Just then he catch sight of Johnny Chuck with every little hair stand up on end and running after Reddy Fox as fast a his short leg could go .
`` Ho !
ho !
ho ! ''
shout Peter Rabbit .
`` Reddy Fox afraid of Johnny Chuck !
Ho !
ho !
Ho ! ''
Then Peter Rabbit scamper away to find Jimmy Skunk and Bobby Coon and Happy Jack Squirrel to tell them all about how Reddy Fox have run away from Johnny Chuck , for you see they be all a little afraid of Reddy Fox .
Straight home run Reddy Fox as fast a he could go , and go home he pass the house of Johnny Chuck .
Now Johnny could n't run so fast a Reddy Fox and he be puff and blow a only a fat little woodchuck can puff and blow when he have to run hard .
Moreover , he have lose his ill temper now and he think it be the best joke ever to think that he have actually frighten Reddy Fox .
When he come to his own house he stop and sit on his hind legs once more .
Then he shrill out after Reddy Fox : `` Reddy Fox be a ` fraid cat , ` fraid-cat !
Reddy Fox be a ` fraid-cat ! ''
And all the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind , who be play on the Green Meadows shout : `` Reddy Fox be a ` fraid-cat , ` fraid-cat ! ''
And this be the way that Reddy Fox be surprise and that Johnny Chuck find his way home .
CHAPTER IV WHY JIMMY SKUNK WEARS STRIPES Jimmy Skunk , a everybody know , wear a striped suit , a suit of black and white .
There be a time , long , long ago , when all the Skunk family wear black .
Very handsome their coat be , too , a beautiful , glossy black .
They be very , very proud of them and take the great care of them , brush them carefully ever so many time a day .
There be a Jimmy Skunk then , just a there be now , and he be head of all the Skunk family .
Now this Jimmy Skunk be very proud and think himself very much of a gentleman .
He be very independent and care for no one .
Like a great many other independent people , he do not always consider the right of others .
Indeed , it be hint in the wood and on the Green Meadows that not all of Jimmy Skunk 's doings would bear the light of day .
It be openly say that he be altogether too fond of prowl about at night , but no one could prove that he be responsible for mischief do in the night , for no one saw him .
You see his coat be so black that in the darkness of the night it be not visible at all .
Now about this time of which I be tell you Mrs. Ruffed Grouse make a nest at the foot of the Great Pine and in it she lay fifteen beautiful buff egg .
Mrs. Grouse be very happy , very happy indeed , and all the little meadow folk who know of her happiness be happy too , for they all love shy , demure , little Mrs. Grouse .
Every morning when Peter Rabbit trot down the Lone Little Path through the wood past the Great Pine he would stop for a few minute to chat with Mrs. Grouse .
Happy Jack Squirrel would bring her the news every afternoon .
The Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind would run up a dozen time a day to see how she be get along .
One morning Peter Rabbit , come down the Lone Little Path for his usual morning call , find a terrible state of affair .
Poor little Mrs. Grouse be heart-broken .
All about the foot of the Great Pine lay the empty shell of her beautiful egg .
They have be break and scatter this way and that .
`` How do it happen ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` I do n't know , '' sob poor little Mrs. Grouse .
`` In the night when I be fast asleep something pounce upon me .
I manage to get away and fly up in the top of the Great Pine .
In the morning I find all my egg break , just a you see them here . ''
Peter Rabbit look the ground over very carefully .
He hunt around behind the Great Pine , he look under the bush , he study the ground with a very wise air .
Then he hop off down the Lone Little Path to the Green Meadows .
He stop at the house of Johnny Chuck .
`` What make your eye so big and round ? ''
ask Johnny Chuck .
Peter Rabbit come very close so a to whisper in Johnny Chuck 's ear , and tell him all that he have see .
Together they go to Jimmy Skunk 's house .
Jimmy Skunk be in bed .
He be very sleepy and very cross when he come to the door .
Peter Rabbit tell him what he have see .
`` Too bad !
Too bad ! ''
say Jimmy Skunk , and yawn sleepily .
`` Wo n't you join u in try to find out who do it ? ''
ask Johnny Chuck .
Jimmy Skunk say he would be delight to come but that he have some other business that morning and that he would join them in the afternoon .
Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck go on .
Pretty soon they meet the Merry Little Breezes and tell them the dreadful story .
`` What shall we do ? ''
ask Johnny Chuck .
`` We 'll hurry over and tell Old Dame Nature , '' cry the Merry Little Breezes , `` and ask her what to do . ''
So away fly the Merry Little Breezes to Old Dame Nature and tell her all the dreadful story .
Old Dame Nature listen very attentively .
Then she send the Merry Little Breezes to all the little meadow folk to tell every one to be at the Great Pine that afternoon .
Now whatever Old Dame Nature command all the meadow folk be oblige to do .
They do not dare to disobey her .
Promptly at four o'clock that afternoon all the meadow folk be gather around the foot of the Great Pine .
Broken-hearted little Mrs. Ruffed Grouse sit beside her empty nest , with all the broken shell about her .
Reddy Fox , Peter Rabbit , Johnny Chuck , Billy Mink , Little Joe Otter , Jerry Muskrat , Hooty the Owl , Bobby Coon , Sammy Jay , Blacky the Crow , Grandfather Frog , Mr. Toad , Spotty the Turtle , the Merry Little Breezes , all be there .
Last of all come Jimmy Skunk .
Very handsome he look in his shin black coat and very sorry he appear that such a dreadful thing should have happen .
He tell Mrs. Grouse how badly he felt , and he loudly demand that the culprit should be find out and severely punish .
Old Dame Nature have the most smiling face in the world , but this time it be very , very grave indeed .
First she ask little Mrs. Grouse to tell her story all over again that all might hear .
Then each in turn be ask to tell where he have be the night before .
Johnny Chuck , Happy Jack Squirrel , Striped Chipmunk , Sammy Jay and Blacky the Crow have go to bed when Mr. Sun go down behind the Purple Hills .
Jerry Muskrat , Billy Mink , Little Joe Otter , Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle have not leave the Smiling Pool .
Bobby Coon have be down in Farmer Brown 's cornfield .
Hooty the Owl have be hunt in the low end of the Green Meadows .
Peter Rabbit have be down in the berry patch .
Mr. Toad have be under the piece of bark which he call a house .
Old Dame Nature call on Jimmy Skunk last of all .
Jimmy protest that he have be very , very tired and have go to bed very early indeed and have sleep the whole night through .
Then Old Dame Nature ask Peter Rabbit what he have find among the egg shell that morning .
Peter Rabbit hop out and lay three long black hair before Old Dame Nature .
`` These , '' say Peter Rabbit `` be what I find among the egg shell . ''
Then Old Dame Nature call Johnny Chuck .
`` Tell u , Johnny Chuck , '' say she , `` what you saw when you call at Jimmy Skunk 's house this morning . ''
`` I saw Jimmy Skunk , '' say Johnny Chuck , `` and Jimmy seem very , very sleepy .
It seem to me that his whisker be yellow . ''
`` That will do , '' say Old Dame Nature , and then she call Old Mother West Wind .
`` What time do you come down on the Green Meadows this morning ? ''
`` Just at the break of day , '' say Old Mother West Wind , `` a Mr. Sun be come up from behind the Purple Hills . ''
`` And whom do you see so early in the morning ? ''
ask Old Dame Nature .
`` I saw Bobby Coon go home from old Farmer Brown 's cornfield , '' say Old Mother West Wind .
`` I saw Hooty the Owl come back from the low end of the Green Meadows .
I saw Peter Rabbit down in the berry patch .
Last of all I saw something like a black shadow come down the Lone Little Path toward the house of Jimmy Skunk . ''
Every one be look very hard at Jimmy Skunk .
Jimmy begin to look very unhappy and very uneasy .
`` Who wear a black coat ? ''
ask Dame Nature .
`` Jimmy Skunk ! ''
shout all the little meadow folk .
`` What MIGHT make whisker yellow ? ''
ask Old Dame Nature .
No one seem to know at first .
Then Peter Rabbit speak up .
`` It MIGHT be the yolk of an egg , '' say Peter Rabbit .
`` Who be likely to be sleepy on a bright sunny morning ? ''
ask Old Dame Nature .
`` People who have be out all night , '' say Johnny Chuck , who himself always go to bed with the sun .
`` Jimmy Skunk , '' say Old Dame Nature , and her voice be very stern , very stern indeed , and her face be very grave .
`` Jimmy Skunk , I accuse you of have break and eat the egg of Mrs. Grouse .
What have you to say for yourself ? ''
Jimmy Skunk hang his head .
He have n't a word to say .
He just want to sneak away by himself .
`` Jimmy Skunk , '' say Old Dame Nature , `` because your handsome black coat of which you be so proud have make it possible for you to move about in the night without be see , and because we can no longer trust you upon your honor , henceforth you and your descendant shall wear a striped coat , which be the sign that you can not be trust .
Your coat hereafter shall be black and white , that when you move about in the night you will always be visible . ''
And this be why that to this day Jimmy Skunk wear a striped suit of black and white .
CHAPTER V THE WILFUL LITTLE BREEZE Old Mother West Wind be tire -- tired and just a wee bit cross -- cross because she be tire .
She have have a very busy day .
Ever since early morning she have be puff out the white sale of the ship on the big ocean so that they could go faster ; she have keep all the big and little wind mill whirl and whirl to pump water for thirsty folk and grind corn for hungry folk ; she have blow away all the smoke from tall chimney and engine and steamboat .
Yes , indeed , Old Mother West Wind have be very , very busy .
Now she be come across the Green Meadows on her way to her home behind the Purple Hills , and a she come she open the big bag she carry and call to her child , the Merry Little Breezes , who have be play hard on the Green Meadows all the long day .
One by one they creep into the big bag , for they be tire , too , and ready to go to their home behind the Purple Hills .
Pretty soon all be in the bag but one , a willful little Breeze , who be not quite ready to go home ; he want to play just a little long .
He dance ahead of Old Mother West Wind .
He kiss the sleepy daisy .
He shake the nodding buttercup .
He set all the little poplar leave a dancing , too , and he would n't come into the big bag .
So Old Mother West Wind close the big bag and slung it over her shoulder .
Then she start on towards her home behind the Purple Hills .
When she have go , the willful little Breeze leave behind suddenly felt very lonely -- very lonely indeed !
The sleepy daisy do n't want to play .
The nodding buttercup be cross .
Great round bright Mr. Sun , who have be shin and shin all day long , go to bed and put on his night cap of golden cloud .
Black shadow come creep , creep out into the Green Meadows .
The willful little Breeze begin to wish that he be safe in Old Mother West Wind 's big bag with all the other Merry Little Breezes .
So he start across the Green Meadows to find the Purple Hills .
But all the hill be black now and he could not tell which he should look behind to find his home with Old Mother West Wind and the Merry Little Breezes .
How he do wish that he have mind Old Mother West Wind .
By and by he curl up under a bayberry bush and try to go to sleep , but he be lonely , oh , so lonely !
And he could n't go to sleep .
Old Mother Moon come up and flood all the Green Meadows with light , but it be n't like the bright light of jolly round Mr. Sun , for it be cold and white and it make many black shadow .
Pretty soon the willful little Breeze heard Hooty the Owl out hunt for a meadow mouse for his dinner .
Then down the Lone Little Path which run close to the bayberry bush trot Reddy Fox .
He be trot very softly and every minute or so he turn his head and look behind him to see if he be follow .
It be plain to see that Reddy Fox be bend on mischief .
When he reach the bayberry bush Reddy Fox sit down and barked twice .
Hooty the Owl answer him at once and fly over to join him .
They do n't see the willful little Breeze curl up under the bayberry bush , so intent be these two rogue in plot mischief .
They be plan to steal down across the Green Meadows to the edge of the Brown Pasture where Mr. Bob White and pretty Mrs. Bob White and a dozen little Bob Whites have their home .
`` When they run along the ground I 'll catch 'em , and when they fly up in the air you 'll catch 'em , and we 'll gobble 'em all up , '' say Reddy Fox to Hooty the Owl .
Then he lick his chop and Hooty the Owl snap his bill , just a if they be taste tender little Bob Whites that very minute .
It make the willful little Breeze shiver to see them .
Pretty soon they start on towards the Brown Pasture .
When they be out of sight the willful little Breeze jump up and shake himself .
Then away he speed across the Green Meadows to the Brown Pasture .
And because he could go faster and because he go a shorter way he get there first .
He have to hunt and hunt to find Mrs. and Mr. Bob White and all the little Bob Whites , but finally he do find them , all with their head tuck under their wing fast asleep .
The willful little Breeze shake Mr. Bob White very gently .
In an instant he be wide awake .
`` Sh-h-h , '' say the willful little Breeze .
`` Reddy Fox and Hooty the Owl be come to the Brown Pasture to gobble up you and Mrs. Bob White and all the little Bob Whites . ''
`` Thank you , little Breeze , '' say Mr. Bob White , `` I think I 'll move my family . ''
Then he wake Mrs. Bob White and all the little Bob Whites .
With Mr. Bob White in the lead away they all fly to the far side of the Brown Pasture where they be soon safely hide under a juniper tree .
The willful little Breeze saw them safely there , and when they be nicely hide hurry back to the place where the Bob Whites have be sleep .
Reddy Fox be steal up through the grass very , very softly .
Hooty the Owl be fly as silently a a shadow .
When Reddy Fox think he be near enough he draw himself together , make a quick spring and land right in Mr. Bob White 's empty bed .
Reddy Fox and Hooty the Owl look so surprised and foolish when they find the Bob Whites be not there that the willful little Breeze nearly laugh out loud .
Then Reddy Fox and Hooty the Owl hunt here and hunt there , all over the Brown Pasture , but they could n't find the Bob Whites .
And the willful little Breeze go back to the juniper tree and curl himself beside Mr. Bob White to sleep , for he be lonely no longer .
CHAPTER VI REDDY FOX GOES FISHING One morning when Mr. Sun be very , very bright and it be very , very warm , down on the Green Meadows Reddy Fox come hop and skip down the Lone Little Path that lead to the Laughing Brook .
Hoppity , skip , skippity hop !
Reddy felt very much please with himself that sunny morning .
Pretty soon he saw Johnny Chuck sit up very straight close by the little house where he live .
`` Johnny Chuck , Chuck , Chuck !
Johnny Chuck , Chuck , Chuck !
Johnny Woodchuck ! ''
call Reddy fox .
Johnny Chuck pretend not to hear .
His mother have tell him not to play with Reddy Fox , for Reddy Fox be a bad boy .
`` Johnny Chuck , Chuck , Chuck !
Johnny Woodchuck ! ''
call Reddy again .
This time Johnny turn and look .
He could see Reddy Fox turn somersault and chase his tail and rolling over and over in the little path .
`` Come on ! ''
say Reddy Fox .
`` Let 's go fishing ! ''
`` Ca n't , '' say Johnny Chuck , because you know , his mother have tell him not to play with Reddy Fox .
`` I 'll show you how to catch a fish , '' say Reddy Fox , and try to jump over his own shadow .
`` Ca n't , '' say good little Johnny Chuck again , and turn away so that he could n't see Reddy Fox chase Butterflies and play catch with Field Mice child .
So Reddy Fox go down to the Laughing Brook all alone .
The Brook be laugh and sing on it way to join the Big River .
The sky be blue and the sun be bright .
Reddy Fox jump on the Big Rock in the middle of the Laughing Brook and peep over the other side .
What do you think he saw ?
Why , right down below in a Dear Little Pool be Mr. And Mrs. Trout and all the little Trouts .
Reddy Fox want some of those little Trouts to take home for his dinner , but he do n't know how to catch them .
He lay flat down on the Big Rock and reach way down into the Dear Little Pool , but all the little Trouts laugh at Reddy Fox and not one come within reach .
Then Mr. Trout swim up so quickly that Reddy Fox do n't see him come and bit Reddy 's little black paw hard .
`` Ouch ! ''
cry Reddy Fox , pull his little black paw out of the water .
And all the little Trouts laugh at Reddy Fox .
Just then along come Billy Mink .
`` Hello , Reddy Fox ! ''
say Billy Mink .
`` What be you do here ? ''
`` I 'm try to catch a fish , '' say Reddy Fox .
`` Pooh !
That 's easy ! ''
say Billy Mink .
`` I 'll show you how . ''
So Billy Mink lay down on the Big Rock side of Reddy Fox and peep over into the Dear Little Pool where all the little Trouts be laugh at Reddy Fox and have such a good time .
But Billy Mink take care , such very great care , that Mr. Trout and Mrs. Trout should not see him peep over into the Dear Little Pool .
When Billy Mink saw all those little Trouts playing in the Dear Little Pool he laugh .
`` You count three , Reddy Fox , '' say he , `` and I 'll show you how to catch a fish . ''
`` One ! ''
say Reddy Fox , `` Two !
Three ! ''
Splash !
Billy Mink have dive head first into the Dear Little Pool .
He spatter water way up onto Reddy Fox , and he frighten old Mr. Frog so that he fell over backwards off the lily pad where he be take a morning nap right into the water .
In a minute Billy Mink climb out on the other side of the Dear Little Pool and sure enough , he have catch one of the little Trouts .
`` Give it to me , '' cry Reddy Fox .
`` Catch one yourself , '' say Billy Mink .
`` Old Grandpa Mink want a fish for his dinner , so I be go to take this home .
You 're afraid , Reddy Fox !
` Fraid-cat !
Fraid-cat ! ''
Billy Mink shake the water off of his little brown coat , pick up the little Trout and run off home .
Reddy Fox lay down again on the Big Rock and peep into the Dear Little Pool .
Not a single Trout could he see .
They be all hide safely with Mr. and Mrs. Trout .
Reddy Fox watch and watch .
The sun be warm , the Laughing Brook be sing a lullaby and -- what do you think ?
Why , Reddy Fox go fast asleep on the edge of the great Big Rock .
By and by Reddy Fox begin to dream .
He dream that he have a nice little brown coat that be waterproof , just like the little brown coat that Billy Mink wore .
Yes , and he dream that he have learn to swim and to catch fish just a Billy Mink do .
He dream that the Dear Little Pool be full of little Trouts and that he be just go to catch one when -- splash !
Reddy Fox have roll right off of the Big Rock into the Dear Little Pool .
The water go into the eye of Reddy Fox , and it go up his nose and he swallow so much that he felt a if he never , never would want another drink of water .
And his beautiful red coat , which old Mother Fox have tell him to be very , very careful of because he could n't have another for a whole year , be oh so wet !
And his pant be wet and his beautiful bushy tail , of which he be so proud , be so full of water that he could n't hold it up , but have to drag it up the bank after him a he crawl out of the Dear Little Pool .
`` Ha !
Ha !
Ha ! ''
laugh Mr. Kingfisher , sit on a tree .
`` Ho !
Ho !
Ho ! ''
laugh old Mr. Frog , who have climb back on his lily pad .
`` He !
He !
He ! ''
laugh all the little Trouts and Mr. Trout and Mrs. Trout , swim round and round in the Dear Little Pool .
`` Ha !
Ha !
Ha !
Ho !
Ho !
Ho !
He !
He !
He ! ''
laugh Billy Mink , who have come back to the Big Rock just in time to see Reddy Fox tumble in .
Reddy Fox do n't say a word , he be so ashamed .
He just creep up the Lone Little Path to his home , drag his tail , all wet and muddy , behind him , and drip water all the way .
Johnny Chuck be still sit by his door a his mother have tell him to .
Reddy Fox try to go past without be see , but Johnny Chuck 's bright little eye saw him .
`` Where be your fish , Reddy Fox ? ''
call Johnny Chuck .
`` Why do n't you turn somersault , and jump over your shadow and chase Butterflies and play with the little Field Mice , Reddy Fox ? ''
call Johnny Chuck .
But Reddy Fox just walk faster .
When he get almost home he saw old Mother Fox sit in the doorway with a great big switch across her lap , for Mother Fox have tell Reddy Fox not to go near the Laughing Brook .
And this be all I be go to tell you about how Reddy Fox go fishing .
CHAPTER VII JIMMY SKUNK LOOKS FOR BEETLES Jimmy Skunk open his eye very early one morning and peep out of his snug little house on the hill .
Big , round Mr. Sun , with a very red , smile face , have just begin to climb up into the sky .
Old Mother West Wind be just start down to the Green Meadows with her big bag over her shoulder .
In that bag Jimmy Skunk know she carry all her child , the Merry Little Breezes , whom she be take down to the Green Meadows to play and frolic all day .
`` Good morning , Mother West Wind , '' say Jimmy Skunk , politely .
`` Did you see any beetle a you come down the hill ? ''
Old Mother West Wind say , no , she have n't see any beetle a she come down the hill .
`` Thank you , '' say Jimmy Skunk politely .
`` I guess I 'll have to go look myself , for I 'm very , very hungry . ''
So Jimmy Skunk brush his handsome black and white coat , and wash his face and hand , and start out to try to find some beetle for his breakfast .
First he go down to the Green Meadows and stop at Johnny Chuck 's house .
But Johnny Chuck be still in bed and fast asleep .
Then Jimmy Skunk go over to see if Reddy Fox would go with him to help find some beetle for his breakfast .
But Reddy Fox have be out very , very late the night before and be still in bed fast asleep , too .
So Jimmy Skunk set out all alone along the Crooked Little Path up the hill to find some beetle for his breakfast .
He walk very slowly , for Jimmy Skunk never hurry .
He stop and peep under every old log to see if there be any beetle .
By and by he come to a big piece of bark beside the Crooked Little Path .
Jimmy Skunk take hold of the piece of bark with his two little black paw and pull and pull .
All of a sudden , the big piece of bark turn over so quickly that Jimmy Skunk fell flat on his back .
When Jimmy Skunk have roll over onto his foot again , there sit old Mr. Toad right in the path , and old Mr. Toad be very , very cross indeed .
He swell and he puff and he puff and he swell , till he be twice as big a Jimmy Skunk have ever see him before .
`` Good morning , Mr. Toad , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` Have you see any beetle ? ''
But Mr. Toad blink his great round goggly eye and he say : `` What do you mean , Jimmy Skunk , by pull the roof off my house ? ''
`` Is that the roof of your house ? ''
ask Jimmy Skunk politely .
`` I wo n't do it again . ''
Then Jimmy Skunk step right over old Mr. Toad , and go on up the Crooked Little Path to look for some beetle .
By and by he come to an old stump of a tree which be hollow and have the nice little round hole in one side .
Jimmy Skunk take hold of one edge with his two little black paw and pull and pull .
All of a sudden the whole side of the old stump tore open and Jimmy Skunk fell flat on his back .
When Jimmy Skunk have roll over onto his foot again there be Striped Chipmunk hop up and down right in the middle of the path , he be so angry .
`` Good morning , Striped Chipmunk , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` Have you see any beetle ? ''
But Striped Chipmunk hop faster than ever and he say : `` What do you mean , Jimmy Skunk , by pull the side off my house ? ''
`` Is that the side of your house ? ''
ask Jimmy Skunk , politely .
`` I wo n't do it again . ''
Then Jimmy Skunk step right over Striped Chipmunk , and go on up the Crooked Little Path to look for some beetle .
Pretty soon he meet Peter Rabbit hop along down the Crooked Little Path .
`` Good morning , Jimmy Skunk , where be you go so early in the morning ? ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` Good morning , Peter Rabbit .
Have you see any beetle ? ''
ask Jimmy Skunk , politely .
`` No , I have n't see any beetle , but I 'll help you find some , '' say Peter Rabbit .
So he turn about and hop ahead of Jimmy Skunk up the Crooked Little Path .
Now because Peter Rabbit 's leg be long and he be always in a hurry , he get to the top of the hill first .
When Jimmy Skunk reach the end of the Crooked Little Path on the top of the hill he find Peter Rabbit sit up very straight and look and look very hard at a great flat stone .
`` What be you look at , Peter Rabbit ? ''
ask Jimmy Skunk .
`` Sh-h-h ! ''
say Peter Rabbit , `` I think there be some beetle under that great flat stone where that little black string be stick out .
Now when I count three you grab that string and pull hard perhaps you 'll find a beetle at the other end . ''
So Jimmy Skunk get ready and Peter Rabbit begin to count .
`` One ! ''
say Peter .
`` Two ! ''
say Peter .
`` Three ! ''
Jimmy Skunk grab the black string and pull as hard a ever he could and out come -- Mr. Black Snake !
The string Jimmy Skunk have pull be Mr. Black Snake 's tail , and Mr. Black Snake be very , very angry indeed .
`` Ha !
Ha !
Ha ! ''
laugh Peter Rabbit .
`` What do you mean , Jimmy Skunk , '' say Mr. Black Snake , `` by pull my tail ? ''
`` Was that your tail ? ''
say Jimmy Skunk , politely .
`` I wo n't do it again .
Have you see any beetle ? ''
But Mr. Black Snake have n't see any beetle , and he be so cross that Jimmy Skunk go on over the hill to look for some beetle .
Peter Rabbit be still laugh and laugh and laugh .
And the more he laugh the angrier grow Mr. Black Snake , till finally he start after Peter Rabbit to teach him a lesson .
Then Peter Rabbit stop laugh , for Mr. Black Snake can run very fast .
Away go Peter Rabbit down the Crooked Little Path a fast a he could go , and away go Mr. Black Snake after him .
But Jimmy Skunk do n't even look once to see if Mr. Black Snake have catch Peter Rabbit to teach him a lesson , for Jimmy Skunk have find some beetle and be eat his breakfast .
CHAPTER VIII BILLY MINK 'S SWIMMING PARTY Billy Mink be come down the bank of the Laughing Brook .
Billy Mink be feel very good indeed .
He have have a good breakfast , the sun be warm , little white cloud ship be sail across the blue sky and their shadow be sail across the Green Meadows , the bird be sing and the bee be hum .
Billy Mink felt like sing too , but Billy Mink 's voice be not mean for singing .
By and by Billy Mink come to the Smiling Pool .
Here the Laughing Brook stop and rest on it way to join the Big River .
It stop it noisy laughing and singing and just lay smile and smile in the warm sunshine .
The little flower on the bank lean over and nod to it .
The beech tree , which be very old , sometimes drop a leaf into it .
The cat-tails keep their foot cool in the edge of it .
Billy Mink jump out on the Big Rock and look down into the Smiling Pool .
Over on a green lily pad he saw old Grandfather Frog .
`` Hello , Grandfather Frog , '' say Billy Mink .
`` Hello , Billy Mink , '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` What mischief be you up to this fine sunny morning ? ''
Just then Billy Mink saw a little brown head swim along one edge of the Smiling Pool .
`` Hello , Jerry Muskrat ! ''
shout Billy Mink .
`` Hello your own self , Billy Mink , '' shout Jerry Muskrat , `` Come in and have a swim ; the water 's fine ! ''
`` Good , '' say Billy Mink .
`` We 'll have a swimming party . ''
So Billy Mink call all the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind , who be play with the flower on the bank , and send them to find Little Joe Otter and invite him to come to the swim party .
Pretty soon back come the Little Breezes and with them come Little Joe Otter .
`` Hello , Billy Mink , '' say Little Joe Otter .
`` Here I be ! ''
`` Hello , Little Joe Otter , '' say Billy Mink .
`` Come up here on the Big Rock and see who can dive the deep into the Smiling Pool . ''
So Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat climb up on the Big Rock side of Billy Mink and they all stand side by side in their little brown bath suit look down into the Smiling Pool .
`` Now when I count three we 'll all dive into the Smiling Pool together and see who can dive the deep .
One ! ''
say Billy Mink .
`` Two ! ''
say Billy Mink .
`` Three ! ''
say Billy Mink .
And when he say `` Three ! ''
in they all go head first .
My such a splash a they do make !
They upset old Grandfather Frog so that he fell off his lily pad .
They frighten Mr. and Mrs. Trout so that they jump right out of the water .
Tiny Tadpole have such a scare that he hide way , way down in the mud with only the tip of his funny little nose stick out .
`` Chug-a-rum , '' say old Grandfather Frog , climb out of his lily pad .
`` If I be n't so old I would show you how to dive . ''
`` Come on , Grandfather Frog ! ''
cry Billy Mink .
`` Show u how to dive . ''
And what do you think ?
Why , old Grandfather Frog actually get so excited that he climb up on the Big Rock to show them how to dive .
Splash !
Went Grandfather Frog into the Smiling Pool .
Splash !
Went Billy Mink right behind him .
Splash !
Splash !
Went Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat , right at Billy Mink 's heel .
`` Hurrah ! ''
shout Mr. Kingfisher , sit on a branch of the old beech tree .
And then just to show them that he could dive , too , splash !
He go into the Smiling Pool .
Such a noise a they do make !
All the Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind dance for joy on the bank .
Blacky the Crow and Sammy Jay fly over to see what be go on .
`` Now let 's see who can swim the farthest under water , '' cry Billy Mink .
So they all stand side by side on one edge of the Smiling Pool .
`` Go ! ''
shout Mr. Kingfisher , and in they all plunge .
Little ripple run across the Smiling Pool and then the water become a smooth and smiling a if nothing have go into it with a plunge .
Now old Grandfather Frog begin to realize that he be n't as young a he use to be , and he could n't swim as fast a the others anyway .
He begin to get short of breath , so he swim up to the top and stuck just the tip of his nose out to get some more air .
Sammy Jay 's sharp eye saw him .
`` There 's Grandfather Frog ! ''
he shout .
So then Grandfather Frog pop his head out and swim over to his green lily pad to rest .
Way over beyond the Big Rock little bubble in three long row keep come up to the top of the Smiling Pool .
They show just where Billy Mink , Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat be swim way down out of sight .
It be the air from their lung make the bubble .
Straight across the Smiling Pool go the line of little bubble and then way out on the farther side two little head bob out of water close together .
They be Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter .
A moment later Jerry Muskrat bob up beside them .
You see , they have swim clear across the Smiling Pool and of course they could swim no farther .
So Billy Mink 's swim party be a great success .
CHAPTER IX PETER RABBIT PLAYS A JOKE One morning when big round Mr. Sun be climb up in the sky and Old Mother West Wind have send all her Merry Little Breezes to play in the Green Meadows , Johnny Chuck start out for a walk .
First he sit up very straight and look and look all around to see if Reddy Fox be anywhere about , for you know Reddy Fox like to tease Johnny Chuck .
But Reddy Fox be nowhere to be see , so Johnny Chuck trot down the Lone Little Path to the wood .
Mr. Sun be shin as brightly a ever he could and Johnny Chuck , who be very , very fat , grow very , very warm .
By and by he sit down on the end of a log under a big tree to rest .
Thump !
Something hit Johnny Chuck right on the top of his round little head .
It make Johnny Chuck jump .
`` Hello , Johnny Chuck ! ''
say a voice that seem to come right out of the sky .
Johnny Chuck tip his head way , way back and look up .
He be just in time to see Happy Jack Squirrel drop a nut .
Down it come and hit Johnny Chuck right on the tip of his funny , black , little nose .
`` Oh ! ''
say Johnny Chuck , and tumble right over back off the log .
But Johnny Chuck be so round and so fat and so roly-poly that it do n't hurt him a bit .
`` Ha !
Ha !
Ha ! ''
laugh Happy Jack up in the tree .
`` Ha !
Ha !
Ha ! ''
laugh Johnny Chuck , pick himself up .
Then they both laugh together .
It be such a good joke .
`` What be you laugh at ? ''
ask a voice so close to Johnny Chuck that he roll over three time he be so surprised .
It be Peter Rabbit .
`` What be you do in my wood ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` I 'm take a walk , '' say Johnny Chuck .
`` Good , '' say Peter Rabbit , `` I 'll come along too . ''
So Johnny Chuck and Peter Rabbit set out along the Lone Little Path through the wood .
Peter Rabbit hop along with great big jump , for Peter 's leg be long and meant for jumping , but Johnny Chuck could n't keep up though he try very hard , for Johnny 's leg be short .
Pretty soon Peter Rabbit come back , walk very softly .
He whisper in Johnny Chuck 's ear .
`` I 've find something , '' say Peter Rabbit .
`` What be it ? ''
ask Johnny Chuck .
`` I 'll show you , '' say Peter Rabbit , `` but you must be very , very still , and not make the least little bit of noise . ''
Johnny Chuck promise to be very , very still for he want very much to see what Peter Rabbit have find .
Peter Rabbit tip-toed down the Lone Little Path through the wood , his funny long ear point right up to the sky .
And behind him tip-toed Johnny Chuck , wonder and wonder what it could be that Peter Rabbit have find .
Pretty soon they come to a nice mossy green log right across the Lone Little Path .
Peter Rabbit stop and sit up very straight .
He look this way and look that way .
Johnny Chuck stop too and he sit up very straight and look this way and look that way , but all he could see be the mossy green log across the Lone Little Path .
`` What be it , Peter Rabbit ? ''
whisper Johnny Chuck .
`` You ca n't see it yet , '' whisper Peter Rabbit , `` for first we have to jump over that mossy green log .
Now I 'll jump first , and then you jump just the way I do , and then you 'll see what it be I 've find , '' say Peter Rabbit .
So Peter Rabbit jump first , and because his leg be long and meant for jumping , he jump way , way over the mossy green log .
Then he turn around and sit up to see Johnny Chuck jump over the mossy green log , too .
Johnny Chuck try to jump very high and very far , just a he have see Peter Rabbit jump , but Johnny Chuck 's leg be very short and not mean for jumping .
Besides , Johnny Chuck be very , very fat .
So though he try very hard indeed to jump just like Peter Rabbit , he stub his toe on the top of the mossy green log and over he tumble , head first , and land with a great big thump right on Reddy Fox , who be lie fast asleep on the other side of the mossy green log .
Peter Rabbit laugh and laugh until he have to hold his side .
My , how frightened Johnny Chuck be when he saw what he have do !
Before he could get on his foot he have roll right over behind a little bush , and there he lay very , very still .
Reddy Fox awake with a grunt when Johnny Chuck fell on him so hard , and the first thing he saw be Peter Rabbit laugh so that he have to hold his side .
Reddy Fox do n't stop to look around .
He think that Peter Rabbit have jump on him .
Up jump Reddy Fox and away run Peter Rabbit .
Away go Reddy Fox after Peter Rabbit .
Peter dodge behind the tree , and jump over the bush , and run this way and run that way , just as hard a ever he could , for Peter Rabbit be very much afraid of Reddy Fox .
And Reddy Fox follow Peter Rabbit behind the tree and over the bush this way and that way , but he could n't catch Peter Rabbit .
Pretty soon Peter Rabbit come to the house of Jimmy Skunk .
He know that Jimmy Skunk be over in the pasture , so he pop right in and then he be safe , for the door of Jimmy Skunk 's house be too small for Reddy Fox to squeeze in .
Reddy Fox sit down and waited , but Peter Rabbit do n't come out .
By and by Reddy Fox give it up and trot off home where old Mother Fox be wait for him .
All this time Johnny Chuck have sit very still , watch Reddy Fox try to catch Peter Rabbit .
And when he saw Peter Rabbit pop into the house of Jimmy Skunk and Reddy Fox trot away home , Johnny Chuck stand up and brush his little coat very clean and then he trot back up the Lone Little Path through the wood to his own dear little path through the Green Meadows where the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind be still play , till he be safe in his own snug little house once more .
CHAPTER X HOW SAMMY JAY WAS FOUND OUT Sammy Jay be very busy , very busy indeed .
When anyone happen that way Sammy Jay pretend to be do nothing at all , for Sammy Jay think himself a very fine gentleman .
He be very proud of his handsome blue coat with white trimming and his high cap , and he would sit on a fence post and make fun of Johnny Chuck work at a new door for his snug little home in the Green Meadows , and of Striped Chipmunk store up heap of corn and nut for the winter , for most of the time Sammy Jay be an idle fellow .
And when Sammy Jay WAS busy , he be pretty sure to be do something that he ought not to do , for idle people almost always get into mischief .
Sammy Jay be in mischief now , and that be why he pretend to be do nothing when he think any one be look .
Old Mother West Wind have come down from her home behind the Purple Hills very early that morning .
Indeed , jolly , round , red Mr. Sun have hardly get out of bed when she cross the Green Meadows on her way to help the big ship across the ocean .
Old Mother West Wind 's eye be sharp , and she saw Sammy Jay before Sammy Jay saw her .
`` Now what can Sammy Jay be so busy about , and why be he so very , very quiet ? ''
think Old Mother West Wind .
`` He must be up to some mischief . ''
So when she open her big bag and turn out all her Merry Little Breezes to play on the Green Meadows she send one of them to see what Sammy Jay be do in the old chestnut tree .
The Merry Little Breeze dance along over the tree top just a if he have n't a think in the world but to wake up all the little leaf and set them to dance too , and Sammy Jay , watch Old Mother West Wind and the other Merry Little Breezes , do n't see this Merry Little Breeze at all .
Pretty soon it dance back to Old Mother West Wind and whisper in her ear : `` Sammy Jay be steal the nut Happy Jack Squirrel have hide in the hollow of the old chestnut tree , and be hide them for himself in the tumble down nest that Blacky the Crow build in the Great Pine last year . ''
`` Aha ! ''
say Old Mother West Wind .
Then she go on across the Green Meadows .
`` Good morning , Old Mother West Wind , '' say Sammy Jay a she pass the fence post where he be sit .
`` Good morning , Sammy Jay , '' say Old Mother West Wind .
`` What bring you out so early in the morning ? ''
`` I 'm out for my health , Old Mother West Wind , '' say Sammy Jay politely .
`` The doctor have order me to take a bath in the dew at sunrise every morning . ''
Old Mother West Wind say nothing , but go on her way across the Green Meadows to blow the ship across the ocean .
When she have pass , Sammy Jay hurry to take the last of Happy Jack 's nut to the old nest in the Great Pine .
Poor Happy Jack !
Soon he come dance along with another nut to put in the hollow of the old chestnut tree .
When he peep in and saw that all his big store of nut have disappear , he could n't believe his own eye .
He put in one paw and felt all around but not a nut could he feel .
Then he climb in and sure enough , the hollow be empty .
Poor Happy Jack !
There be tear in his eye when he creep out again .
He look all around but no one be to be see but handsome Sammy Jay , very busy brush his beautiful blue coat .
`` Good morning , Sammy Jay , have you see any one pas this way ? ''
ask Happy Jack .
`` Some one have steal a store of nut from the hollow in the old chestnut tree . ''
Sammy Jay pretend to feel very badly indeed , and in his sweet voice , for his voice be very sweet in those day , he offer to help Happy Jack try to catch the thief who have steal the store of nut from the hollow in the old chestnut tree .
Together they go down cross the Green Meadows ask every one whom they meet if they have see the thief who have steal Happy Jack 's store of nut from the hollow in the old chestnut tree .
All the Merry Little Breezes join in the search , and soon every one who live in the Green Meadows or in the wood know that some one have steal all of Happy Jack Squirrel 's store of nut from the hollow in the old chestnut tree .
And because every one like Happy Jack , every one felt very sorry indeed for him .
The next morning all the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind be turn out of the big bag into the Green Meadows very early indeed , for they have a lot of errand to do .
All over the Green Meadows they hurry , all through the wood , up and down the Laughing Brook and all around the Smiling Pool , invite everybody to meet at the Great Pine on the hill at nine o'clock to form a committee of the whole -- to try to find the thief who steal Happy Jack 's nut from the hollow in the old chestnut tree .
And because every one like Happy Jack every one go to the Great Pine on the hill -- Reddy Fox , Bobby Coon , Jimmy Skunk Striped Chipmunk , who be Happy Jack 's cousin you know , Billy Mink , Little Joe Otter , Jerry Muskrat , Hooty the Owl , who be almost too sleepy to keep his eye open , Blacky the Crow , Johnny Chuck , Peter Rabbit , even old Grandfather Frog .
Of course Sammy Jay be there , look his handsomest .
When they have all gather around the Great Pine , Old Mother West Wind point to the old nest way up in the top of it .
`` Is that your nest ? ''
she ask Blacky the Crow .
`` It be , but I give it to my cousin , Sammy Jay , '' say Blacky the Crow .
`` Is that your nest , and may I have a stick out of it ? ''
ask Old Mother West Wind of Sammy Jay .
`` It be , '' say Sammy Jay , with his politest bow , `` And you be welcome to a stick out of it . ''
To himself he think , `` She will only take one from the top and that wo n't matter . ''
Old Mother West Wind suddenly puff out her cheek and blow so hard that she blow a big stick right out of the bottom of the old nest .
Down it fell bumpity-bump on the branch of the Great Pine .
After it fell -- what do you think ?
Why , hickory nut and chestnut and acorn and hazel nut , such a lot of them !
`` Why !
Why -- e -- e ! '' cry Happy Jack .
`` There be all my steal nut ! ''
Everybody turn to look at Sammy Jay , but he be fly off through the wood as fast a he could go .
`` Stop thief ! ''
cry Old Mother West Wind .
`` Stop thief ! ''
cry all the Merry Little Breezes and Johnny Chuck and Billy Mink and all the rest .
But Sammy Jay do n't stop .
Then all begin to pick up the nut that have fall from the old nest where Sammy Jay have hide them .
By and by , with Happy Jack lead the way , they all march back to the old chestnut tree and there Happy Jack store all the nut away in his snug little hollow once more .
And ever since that day , Sammy Jay , whenever he try to call , just scream : `` Thief ! ''
`` Thief ! ''
`` Thief ! ''
CHAPTER XI JERRY MUSKRAT 'S PARTY All the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind be hurry over the Green Meadows .
Some fly this way and some run that way and some dance the other way .
You see , Jerry Muskrat have ask them to carry his invitation to a party at the Big Rock in the Smiling Pool .
Of course every one say that they would be delight to go to Jerry Muskrat 's party .
Round Mr. Sun shine his very bright .
The sky be it blue and the little bird have promise to be there to sing for Jerry Muskrat , so of course all the little folk in the Green Meadows and in the wood want to go .
There be Johnny Chuck and Reddy Fox and Jimmy Skunk and Bobby Coon and Happy Jack Squirrel and Striped Chipmunk and Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Grandfather Frog and old Mr. Toad and Mr. Blacksnake -- all go to Jerry Muskrat 's party .
When they reach the Smiling Pool they find Jerry Muskrat all ready .
His brother and his sister , his aunt and his uncle and his cousin be all there .
Such a merry , merry time a there be in the Smiling Pool !
How the water do splash !
Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Grandfather Frog jump right in as soon a they get there .
They play tag in the water and hid behind the Big Rock .
They turn somersault down the slippery slide and they have such a good time !
But Reddy Fox and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon and Johnny Chuck and Jimmy Skunk and Happy Jack and Striped Chipmunk could n't swim , so of course they could n't play tag in the water or hide and seek or go down the slippery slide ; all they could do be sit around to look on and wish that they know how to swim , too .
So of course they do n't have a good time .
Soon they begin to wish that they have n't come to Jerry Muskrat 's party .
When he find that they be not have a good time , poor Jerry Muskrat felt very badly indeed .
You see he live in the water so much that he have quite forget that there be anyone who could n't swim , or he never , never would have invite all the little meadow folk who live on dry land .
`` Let 's go home , '' say Peter Rabbit to Johnny Chuck .
`` We can have more fun up on the hill , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
Just then Little Joe Otter come push a great big log across the Smiling Pool .
`` Here 's a ship , Bobby Coon .
You get on one end and I 'll give you a sail across the Smiling Pool , '' shout Little Joe Otter .
So Bobby Coon crawl out on the big log and hold on very tight , while little Joe Otter swam behind and push the big log .
Across the Smiling Pool they go and back again .
Bobby Coon have such a good ride that he want to go again , but Jimmy Skunk want a ride .
So Bobby Coon hop off of the big log and Jimmy Skunk hop on and away he go across the Smiling Pool with little Joe Otter push behind .
Then Jerry Muskrat find another log and give Peter Rabbit a ride .
Jerry Muskrat 's brother and sister and aunt and uncle and cousin find log and take Reddy Fox and Johnny Chuck and even Mr. Toad back and forth across the Smiling Pool .
Happy Jack Squirrel sit up very straight on the end of his log and spread his great bushy tail for a sail .
All the little Breezes blew and blew and Happy Jack Squirrel sail round and round the Smiling Pool .
Sometimes someone would fall off into the water and get wet , but Jerry Muskrat or Billy Mink always pull them out again , and no one care the tiny bit for a wetting .
In the bush around the Smiling Pool the little bird sang and sang .
Reddy Fox bark his loud .
Happy Jack Squirrel chatter and chir -- r -- r -- ed .
All the muskrat squeal and squeak , for Jerry Muskrat 's party be such fun !
By and by when Mr. Sun go down behind the Purple Hills to his home and Old Mother West Wind with all her Merry Little Breezes go after him , and the little star come out to twinkle and twinkle , the Smiling Pool lay all quiet and still , but smile and smile to think what a good time every one have have at Jerry Muskrat 's party .
CHAPTER XII BOBBY COON AND REDDY FOX PLAY TRICKS It be night .
All the little star be look down and twinkle and twinkle .
Mother Moon be do her best to make the Green Meadows as light a Mr. Sun do in the daytime .
All the little bird except Hooty the Owl and Boomer the Night Hawk , and noisy Mr. Whip-poor-will be fast asleep in their little nest .
Old Mother West Wind 's Merry Little Breezes have all go to sleep , too .
It be oh so still !
Indeed it be so very still that Bobby Coon , come down the Lone Little Path through the wood , begin to talk to himself .
`` I do n't see what people want to play all day and sleep all night for , '' say Bobby Coon .
`` Night 's the best time to be about .
Now Reddy Fox -- '' `` Be careful what you say about Reddy Fox , '' say a voice right behind Bobby Coon .
Bobby Coon turn around very quickly indeed , for he have think he be all alone .
There be Reddy Fox himself , trot down the Lone Little Path through the wood .
`` I think you be home and fast asleep , Reddy Fox , '' say Bobby Coon .
`` You be mistake , '' say Reddy Fox .
`` For you see I 'm out to take a walk in the moonlight . ''
So Bobby Coon and Reddy Fox walk together down the Lone Little Path through the wood to the Green Meadows .
They meet Jimmy Skunk , who have dream that there be a lot of beetle up on the hill , and be just go to climb the Crooked Little Path to see .
`` Hello , Jimmy Skunk ! ''
say Bobby Coon and Reddy Fox .
`` Come down to the Green Meadows with u . ''
Jimmy Skunk say he would , so they all go down on the Green Meadows together , Bobby Coon first , Reddy Fox next and Jimmy Skunk last of all , for Jimmy Skunk never hurry .
Pretty soon they come to the house of Johnny Chuck .
`` Listen , '' say Bobby Coon .
`` Johnny Chuck be fast asleep . ''
They all listen and they could hear Johnny Chuck snore away down in his snug little bed .
`` Let 's give Johnny Chuck a surprise , '' say Reddy Fox .
`` What shall it be ? ''
ask Bobby Coon .
`` I know , '' say Reddy Fox .
`` Let 's roll that big stone right over Johnny Chuck 's doorway ; then he 'll have to dig his way out in the morning . ''
So Bobby Coon and Reddy Fox pull and tug and tug and pull at the big stone till they have roll it over Johnny Chuck 's doorway .
Jimmy Skunk pretend not to see what they be do .
`` Now let 's go down to the Laughing Brook and wake up old Grandfather Frog and hear him say ` Chug-a-rum , ' '' say Bobby Coon .
`` Come on ! ''
cry Reddy Fox , `` I 'll get there first ! ''
Away race Reddy Fox down the Lone Little Path and after him run Bobby Coon , go to wake old Grandfather Frog from a nice comfortable sleep on his green lily pad .
But Jimmy Skunk do n't go .
He watch Reddy Fox and Bobby Coon until they be nearly to the Laughing Brook .
Then he begin to dig at one side of the big stone which fill the doorway of Johnny Chuck 's house .
My , how he make the dirt fly !
Pretty soon he have make a hole big enough to call through to Johnny Chuck , who be snore away , fast asleep in his snug little bed below .
`` Johnny Chuck , Chuck , Chuck !
Johnny Woodchuck ! ''
call Jimmy Skunk .
But Johnny Chuck just snore .
`` Johnny Chuck , Chuck , Chuck !
Johnny Woodchuck ! ''
call Jimmy Skunk once more .
But Johnny Chuck just snore .
Then Jimmy Skunk call again , this time loud than before .
`` Who be it ? ''
ask a very sleepy voice .
`` It 's Jimmy Skunk .
Put your coat on and come up here ! ''
call Jimmy Skunk .
`` Go away , Jimmy Skunk .
I want to sleep ! ''
say Johnny Chuck .
`` I 've get a surprise for you , Johnny Chuck .
You 'd better come ! ''
call Jimmy Skunk through the little hole he have make .
When Johnny Chuck hear that Jimmy Skunk have a surprise for him he want to know right away what it could be , so though he be very , very sleepy , he put on his coat and start up for his door to see what the surprise be that Jimmy Skunk have .
And there he find the big stone Reddy Fox and Bobby Coon have put there , and of course he be very much surprise indeed .
He think Jimmy Skunk have play him a mean trick and for a few minute he be very mad .
But Jimmy Skunk soon tell him who have fill up his doorway with the big stone .
`` Now you push from that side , Johnny Chuck , and I 'll pull from this side , and we 'll soon have this big stone out of your doorway , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
So Johnny Chuck push and Jimmy Skunk pull , and sure enough they soon have the big stone out of Johnny Chuck 's doorway .
`` Now , '' say Jimmy Skunk , `` we 'll roll this big stone down the Lone Little Path to Reddy Fox 's house and we 'll give Reddy Fox a surprise . ''
So Johnny Chuck and Jimmy Skunk tug and pull and roll the big stone down to the house of Reddy Fox , and sure enough , it fill his doorway .
`` Good night , Jimmy Skunk , '' say Johnny Chuck , and trot down the Lone Little Path toward home , chuckle to himself all the way .
Jimmy Skunk walk slowly up the Lone Little Path to the wood , for Jimmy Skunk never hurry .
Pretty soon he come to the big hollow tree where Bobby Coon live , and there he meet Hooty the Owl .
`` Hello , Jimmy Skunk , where have you be ? ''
ask Hooty the Owl .
`` Just for a walk , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` Who live in this big hollow tree ? ''
Now of course Jimmy Skunk know all the time , but he pretend he do n't .
`` Oh , this be Bobby Coon 's house , '' say Hooty the Owl .
`` Let 's give Bobby Coon a surprise , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` How ? ''
ask Hooty the Owl .
`` We 'll fill his house full of stick and leaf , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
Hooty the Owl think that would be a good joke so while Jimmy Skunk gather all the old stick and leave he could find , Hooty the Owl stuff them into the old hollow tree which be Bobby Coon 's house , until he could n't get in another one .
`` Good night , '' say Jimmy Skunk a he begin to climb the Crooked Little Path up the hill to his own snug little home .
`` Good night , '' say Hooty the Owl , a he fly like a big soft shadow over to the Great Pine .
By and by when old Mother Moon be just go to bed and all the little star be too sleepy to twinkle any long , Reddy Fox and Bobby Coon , very tired and very wet from play in the Laughing Brook , come up the Lone Little Path , ready to tumble into their snug little bed .
They be chuckle over the trick they have play on Johnny Chuck , and the way they have wake up old Grandfather Frog , and all the other mischief they have do .
What do you suppose they say when they reach their home and find that someone else have be play joke , too ?
I 'm sure I do n't know , but round , red Mr. Sun be laugh very hard a he peep over the hill at Reddy Fox and Bobby Coon , and he wo n't tell why .
CHAPTER XIII JOHNNY CHUCK FINDS THE BEST THING IN THE WORLD Old Mother West Wind have stop to talk with the Slender Fir Tree .
`` I 've just come across the Green Meadows , '' say Old Mother West Wind , `` and there I saw the Best Thing in the World . ''
Striped Chipmunk be sit under the Slender Fir Tree and he could n't help hear what Old Mother West Wind say .
`` The Best Thing in the World -- now what can that be ? ''
thought Striped Chipmunk .
`` Why , it must be heap and heap of nut and acorn !
I 'll go and find it . ''
So Striped Chipmunk start down the Lone Little Path through the wood as fast a he could run .
Pretty soon he meet Peter Rabbit .
`` Where be you go in such a hurry , Striped Chipmunk ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` Down in the Green Meadows to find the Best Thing in the World , '' reply Striped Chipmunk , and run faster .
`` The Best Thing in the World , '' say Peter Rabbit .
`` Why , that must be great pile of carrot and cabbage !
I think I 'll go and find it . ''
So Peter Rabbit start down the Lone Little Path through the wood as fast a he could go after Striped Chipmunk .
As they pass the great hollow tree Bobby Coon put his head out .
`` Where be you go in such a hurry ? ''
ask Bobby Coon .
`` Down in the Green Meadows to find the Best Thing in the World ! ''
shout Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit , and both begin to run faster .
`` The Best Thing in the World , '' say Bobby Coon to himself .
`` Why , that must be a whole field of sweet milky corn .
I think I 'll go and find it . ''
So Bobby Coon climb down out of the great hollow tree and start down the Lone Little Path through the wood as fast a he could go after Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit , for there be nothing that Bobby Coon like to eat so well a sweet milky corn .
At the edge of the wood they meet Jimmy Skunk .
`` Where be you go in such a hurry ? ''
ask Jimmy Skunk .
`` Down in the Green Meadows to find the Best Thing in the World ! ''
shout Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon .
Then they all try to run faster .
`` The Best Thing in the World , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` Why , that must be pack and pack of beetle ! ''
And for once in his life Jimmy Skunk begin to hurry down the Lone Little Path after Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon .
They be all run so fast that they do n't see Reddy Fox until he jump out of the long grass and ask : `` Where be you go in such a hurry ? ''
`` To find the Best Thing in the World ! ''
shout Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon and Jimmy Skunk , and each do his best to run faster .
`` The Best Thing in the World , '' say Reddy Fox to himself .
`` Why , that must be a whole pen full of tender young chicken , and I must have them . ''
So away go Reddy Fox as fast a he could run down the Lone Little Path after Striped Chipmunk , Peter Rabbit , Bobby Coon and Jimmy Skunk .
By and by they all come to the house of Johnny Chuck .
`` Where be you go in such a hurry ? ''
ask Johnny Chuck .
`` To find the Best Thing in the World , '' shout Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon and Jimmy Skunk and Reddy Fox .
`` The Best Thing in the World , '' say Johnny Chuck .
`` Why , I do n't know of anything good than my own little home and the warm sunshine and the beautiful blue sky . ''
So Johnny Chuck stay at home and play all day among the flower with the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind and be as happy a could be .
But all day long Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon and Jimmy Skunk and Reddy Fox run this way and run that way over the Green Meadows try to find the Best Thing in the World .
The sun be very , very warm and they run so far and they run so fast that they be very , very hot and tired , and still they have n't find the Best Thing in the World .
When the long day be over they start up the Lone Little Path past Johnny Chuck 's house to their own home .
They do n't hurry now for they be so very , very tired !
And they be cross -- oh so cross !
Striped Chipmunk have n't find a single nut .
Peter Rabbit have n't find so much a the leaf of a cabbage .
Bobby Coon have n't find the tiny bit of sweet milky corn .
Jimmy Skunk have n't see a single beetle .
Reddy Fox have n't hear so much a the peep of a chicken .
And all be as hungry a hungry could be .
Half way up the Lone Little Path they meet Old Mother West Wind go to her home behind the hill .
`` Did you find the Best Thing in the World ? ''
ask Old Mother West Wind .
`` NO ! ''
shout Striped Chipmunk and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon and Jimmy Skunk and Reddy Fox all together .
`` Johnny Chuck have it , '' say Old Mother West Wind .
`` It be be happy with the thing you have and not want thing which some one else have .
And it be call Con-tent-ment . ''
CHAPTER XIV LITTLE JOE OTTER 'S SLIPPERY SLIDE Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink have be play together around the Smiling Pool all one sunshiny morning .
They have be fish and have take home a fine dinner of Trout for old Grandfather Mink and blind old Granny Otter .
They have play tag with the Merry Little Breezes .
They have be in all kind of mischief and now they just do n't know what to do .
They be sit side by side on the Big Rock try to push each other off into the Smiling Pool .
Round , smile red Mr. Sun make the Green Meadows very warm indeed , and Reddy Fox , over in the tall grass , hear them splash and shout and have such a good time that he wish he like the nice cool water and could swim , too .
`` I 've think of something ! ''
cry Little Joe Otter .
`` What be it ? ''
ask Billy Mink .
Little Joe Otter just look wise and say nothing .
`` Something to eat ? ''
ask Billy Mink .
`` No , '' say Little Joe Otter .
`` I do n't believe you 've a thought of anything at all , '' say Billy Mink .
`` I have too ! ''
say Little Joe Otter .
`` It 's something to do . ''
`` What ? ''
demand Billy Mink .
Just then Little Joe Otter spy Jerry Muskrat .
`` Hi , Jerry Muskrat !
Come over here ! ''
he call .
Jerry Muskrat swim across to the Big Rock and climb up beside Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter .
`` What be you fellows do ? ''
ask Jerry Muskrat .
`` Having some fun , '' say Billy Mink .
`` Little Joe Otter have think of something to do , but I do n't know what it be . ''
`` Let 's make a slide , '' cry Little Joe Otter .
`` You show u how , '' say Billy Mink .
So Little Joe Otter find a nice smooth place on the bank , and Billy Mink and Jerry Muskrat bring mud and help him pat it down smooth until they have the lovely slippery slide in the world .
Then Little Joe Otter climb up the bank to the top of the slippery slide and lay down flat on his stomach .
Billy Mink give a push and away he go down , down the slippery slide , splash into the Smiling Pool .
Then Jerry Muskrat try it and after him Billy Mink .
Then all do it over again .
Sometimes they go down the slippery slide on their back , sometimes flat on their stomach , sometimes head first , sometimes foot first .
Oh such fun a they do have !
Even Grandfather Frog come over and try the slippery slide .
Johnny Chuck , over in the Green Meadows , hear the noise and steal down the Lone Little Path to see .
Jimmy Skunk , look for beetle up on the hill , hear the noise and forget that he have n't have his breakfast .
Reddy Fox , take a nap , wake up and hurry over to watch the fun .
Last of all come Peter Rabbit .
Little Joe Otter saw him come .
`` Hello , Peter Rabbit ! ''
he shout .
`` Come and try the slippery slide . ''
Now Peter Rabbit could n't swim , but he pretend that he do n't want to .
`` I 've leave my bathing suit at home , '' say Peter Rabbit .
`` Never mind , '' say Billy Mink .
`` Mr. Sun will dry you off . ''
`` And we 'll help , '' say all the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind .
But Peter Rabbit shake his head and say , `` No . ''
Faster and faster go Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat and old Grandfather Frog down the slippery slide into the Smiling Pool .
Peter Rabbit keep come nearer and nearer until finally he stand right at the top of the slippery slide .
Billy Mink creep up behind him very softly and give him a push .
Peter Rabbit 's long leg fly out from under him and down he sit with a thump on the slippery slide .
`` Oh , '' cry Peter Rabbit , and try to stop himself .
But he could n't do it and so away he go down the slippery slide , splash into the Smiling Pool .
`` Ha !
ha !
ha ! ''
laugh Billy Mink .
`` Ho !
ho !
ho ! ''
shout Little Joe Otter .
`` He !
he !
he ! ''
laugh Jerry Muskrat and old Grandfather Frog and Sammy Jay and Jimmy Skunk and Reddy Fox and Blacky the Crow and Mr. Kingfisher , for you know Peter Rabbit be forever play joke on them .
Poor Peter Rabbit !
The water get in his eye and up his nose and into his mouth and make him choke and splutter , and then he could n't get back on the bank , for you know Peter Rabbit could n't swim .
When Little Joe Otter saw what a dreadful time Peter Rabbit be have he dive into the Smiling Pool and take hold of one of Peter Rabbit 's long ear .
Billy Mink swim out and take hold of the other long ear .
Jerry Muskrat swim right under Peter Rabbit and take him on his back .
Then with old Grandfather Frog swim ahead they take Peter Rabbit right across the Smiling Pool and pull him out on the grassy bank , where it be nice and warm .
All the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind come over and help Mr. Sun dry Peter Rabbit off .
Then they all sit down together and watch Little Joe Otter turn a somersault down the slippery slide .
CHAPTER XV THE TAIL OF TOMMY TROUT WHO DID NOT MIND In the Laughing Brook , which ripple and sings all day long , live Mr. Trout and Mrs. Trout , and a whole lot of little Trouts .
There be so many little Trouts that Mr. Trout and Mrs. Trout be keep very busy indeed get breakfast and dinner and supper for them , and watch out for them and teach them how to swim and how to catch foolish little fly that sometimes fell on the water and how to keep out of the way of big hungry fish and sharp eyed Mr. Kingfisher and big men and little boy who come fish with hook and line .
Now all the little Trouts be very , very good and mind just what Mrs. Trout tell them -- all but Tommy Trout , for Tommy Trout -- oh , dear , dear !
Tommy Trout never could mind right away .
He always have to wait a little instead of mind when he be speak to .
Tommy Trout do n't mean to be bad .
Oh dear , no !
He just want to have his own way , and because Tommy Trout have his own way and do n't mind Mrs. Trout there be n't any Tommy Trout now .
No sir , there be n't as much a one little blue spot of his beautiful little coat leave because -- why , just because Tommy Trout do n't mind .
One day when round , red Mr. Sun be shin and the Laughing Brook be sing on it way to join the Big River , Mrs. Trout start to get some nice plump fly for dinner .
All the little Trouts be play in their dear little pool , safe behind the Big Rock .
Before she start Mrs. Trout call all the little Trouts around her and tell them not to leave their little pool while she be go , `` For , '' say she , `` something dreadful might happen to you . ''
All the little Trouts , except Tommy Trout , promise that they would surely , surely stay inside their dear little pool .
Then they all begin to jump and chase each other and play as happy a could be , all but Tommy Trout .
As soon a Mrs. Trout have start , Tommy Trout swim off by himself to the edge of the pool .
`` I wonder what be on the other side of the Big Rock , '' say Tommy Trout .
`` The sun be shin and the brook be laugh and nothing could happen if I go just a little speck of a way . ''
So , when no one be look , Tommy Trout slip out of the safe little pool where all the other little Trouts be play .
He swim just a little speck of a way far still .
Now he could see almost around the Big Rock .
Then he swim just a little speck of a way far and -- oh dear , dear !
he look right into the mouth of a great big , big fish call Mr. Pickerel , who be very fond of little Trouts and would like to eat one for breakfast every day .
`` Ah ha ! ''
say Mr. Pickerel , open his big , big mouth very , very wide .
Tommy Trout turn to run back to the dear , dear safe little pool where all the other little Trouts be play so happily , but he be too late .
Into that great big , big mouth he go instead , and Mr. Pickerel swallow him whole .
`` Ah ha , '' say Mr. Pickerel , `` I like little Trouts . ''
And nothing more be ever hear of Tommy Trout , who do n't mind .
CHAPTER XVI SPOTTY THE TURTLE WINS A RACE All the little people who live on the Green Meadows and in the Smiling Pool and along the Laughing Brook be to have a holiday .
The Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind have be very busy , oh very busy indeed , in send word to all the little meadow folk .
You see , Peter Rabbit have be boast of how fast he could run .
Reddy Fox be quite sure that he could run fast than Peter Rabbit .
Billy Mink , who can move so quickly you hardly can see him , be quite sure that neither Peter Rabbit nor Reddy Fox could run as fast a he .
They all meet one day beside the Smiling Pool and agree that old Grandfather Frog should decide who be the swift .
Now Grandfather Frog be account very wise .
You see he have live a long time , oh , very much long than any of the others , and therefore , because of the wisdom of age , Grandfather Frog be always call on to decide all dispute .
He sit on his green lily-pad while Billy Mink sit on the Big Rock , and Peter Rabbit and Reddy Fox sit on the bank .
Each in turn tell why he think he be the fast .
Old Grandfather Frog listen and listen and say never a word until they be all through .
When they have finish , he stop to catch a foolish green fly and then he say : `` The best way to decide who be the swiftest be to have a race . ''
So it be agree that Peter Rabbit and Reddy Fox and Billy Mink should start together from the old butternut tree on one edge of the Green Meadows , race away across the Green Meadows to the little hill on the other side and each bring back a nut from the big hickory which grow there .
The one who first reach the old butternut tree with a hickory nut would be declare the winner .
The Merry Little Breezes fly about over the Green Meadows tell everyone about the race and everyone plan to be there .
It be a beautiful summer day .
Mr. Sun smile and smile , and the more he smile the warmer it grow .
Everyone be there to see the race -- Striped Chipmunk , Happy Jack Squirrel , Sammy Jay , Blacky the Crow , Hooty the Owl and Bobby Coon all sit up in the old butternut tree where it be cool and shady .
Johnny Chuck , Jerry Muskrat , Jimmy Skunk , Little Joe Otter , Grandfather Frog and even old Mr. Toad , be there .
Last of all come Spotty the Turtle .
Now Spotty the Turtle be a very slow walker , and he can not run at all .
When Peter Rabbit saw him come up towards the old butternut tree he shout : `` Come , Spotty , do n't you want to race with u ? ''
Everybody laugh because you know Spotty be so very , very slow but Spotty do n't laugh and he do n't get cross because everyone else laugh .
`` There be a wise old saying , Peter Rabbit , '' say Spotty the Turtle , `` which show that those who run fast do not always reach a place first .
I think I WILL enter this race . ''
Every one thought that that be the best joke they have hear for a long time , and all laugh hard than ever .
They all agree that Spotty the Turtle should start in the race too .
So they all stand in a row , Peter Rabbit first , the Billy Mink , then Reddy Fox , and right side of Reddy Fox Spotty the Turtle .
`` Are you ready ? ''
ask Grandfather Frog .
`` Go ! ''
Away go Peter Rabbit with great big jump .
After him go Billy Mink so fast that be just a little brown streak go through the tall grass , and side by side with him run Reddy Fox .
Now just a they start Spotty the Turtle reach up and grab the long hair on the end of Reddy 's big tail .
Of course Reddy could n't have stop to shake him off , because Peter Rabbit and Billy Mink be run so fast that he have to run his very best to keep up with them .
But he do n't even know that Spotty the Turtle be there .
You see Spotty be not very heavy and Reddy Fox be so excited that he do not notice that his big tail be heavy than usual .
