The Merry Little Breezes fly along , too , to see that the race be fair .
Peter Rabbit go with great big jump .
Whenever he come to a little bush he jump right over it , for Peter Rabbit 's leg be long and meant for jumping .
Billy Mink be so slim that he slip between the bush and through the long grass like a little brown streak .
Reddy Fox , who be big than either Peter Rabbit or Billy Mink , have no trouble in keep up with them .
Not one of them notice that Spotty the Turtle be hang fast to the end of Reddy 's tail .
Now just at the foot of the little hill on which the big hickory tree grow be a little pond .
It be n't very wide but it be quite long .
Billy Mink remember this pond and he chuckle to himself a he race along , for he know that Peter Rabbit could n't swim and he know that Reddy Fox do not like the water , so therefore both would have to run around it .
He himself can swim even faster than he can run .
The more he think of this , the more foolish it seem that he should hurry so on such a warm day .
`` For , '' say Billy Mink to himself , `` even if they reach the pond first , they will have to run around it , while I can swim across it and cool off while I be swim .
I will surely get there first . ''
So Billy Mink run slow and slow , and pretty soon he have drop behind .
Mr. Sun , round and red , look down , smiled and smile to see the race .
The more he smile the warmer it grow .
Now , Peter Rabbit have a thick gray coat and Reddy Fox have a thick red coat , and they both begin to get very , very warm .
Peter Rabbit do not make such long jump a when he first start .
Reddy Fox begin to feel very thirsty , and his tongue hung out .
Now that Billy Mink be behind them they think they do not need to hurry so .
Peter Rabbit reach the little pond first .
He have not think of that pond when he agree to enter the race .
He stop right on the edge of it and sit up on his hind leg .
Right across he could see the big hickory tree , so near and yet so far , for he know that he must run around the pond then back again , and it be a long , long way .
In just a moment Reddy Fox run out of the bush and Reddy felt much a Peter Rabbit do .
Way , way behind them be Billy Mink , trot along comfortably and chuckle to himself .
Peter Rabbit look at Reddy Fox in dismay , and Reddy Fox look at Peter Rabbit in dismay .
Then they both look at Billy Mink and remember that Billy Mink could swim right across .
Then off Peter Rabbit start as fast a he could go around the pond one way , and Reddy Fox start around the pond the other way .
They be so excited that neither notice a little splash in the pond .
That be Spotty the Turtle who have let go of Reddy 's tail and now be swim across the pond , for you know that Spotty be a splendid swimmer .
Only once or twice he stick his little black nose up to get some air .
The rest of the time he swim under water and no one but the Merry Little Breezes saw him .
Right across he swim , and climb up the bank right under the big hickory tree .
Now there be just three nut leave under the hickory tree .
Two of these Spotty take down to the edge of the pond and bury in the mud .
The other he take in his mouth and start back across the pond .
Just a he reach the other shore up trot Billy Mink , but Billy Mink do n't see Spotty .
He be too intent watch Reddy Fox and Peter Rabbit , who be now half way around the pond .
In he jump with a splash .
My !
How good that cool water do feel !
He do n't have to hurry now , because he felt sure that the race be his .
So he swim round and round and chase some fish and have a beautiful time in the water .
By and by he look up and saw that Peter Rabbit be almost around the pond one way and Reddy Fox be almost around the pond the other way .
They both look tired and hot and discourage .
Then Billy Mink swim slowly across and climb out on the bank under the big hickory tree .
But where be the nut ?
Look a he would , he could not see a nut anywhere , yet the Merry Little Breezes have say there be three nut lie under the hickory tree .
Billy Mink run this way and run that way .
He be still run around , poke over the leaf and look under the twig and piece of bark when Peter Rabbit and Reddy Fox come up .
Then they , too , begin to look under the leaf and under the bark .
They paw around in the grass , they hunt in every nook and cranny , but not a nut could they find .
They be tire and cross and hot and they accuse Billy Mink of have hide the nut .
Billy Mink stoutly insist that he have not hide the nut , that he have not find the nut , and when they saw how hard he be hunt they believe him .
All the afternoon they hunt and hunt and hunt , and all the afternoon Spotty the Turtle , with the nut in his mouth , be slowly , oh , so slowly , crawl straight back across the Green Meadows towards the old butternut tree .
Round , red Mr. Sun be get very close to the Purple Hills , where he go to bed every night , and all the little meadow folk be get ready to go to their home .
They be wonder and wonder what could have happen to the racer , when Sammy Jay spy the Merry Little Breezes dance across the Green Meadows .
`` Here come the Merry Little Breezes ; they 'll tell u who win the race , '' cry Sammy Jay .
When the Merry Little Breezes reach the old butternut tree , all the little meadow folk crowd around them , but the Merry Little Breezes just laugh and laugh and would n't say a word .
Then all of a sudden , out of the tall meadow grass crept Spotty the Turtle and lay the hickory nut at the foot of old Grandfather Frog .
Old Grandfather Frog be so surprised that he actually let a great green fly buzz right past his nose .
`` Where do you get that hickory nut ? ''
ask Grandfather Frog .
`` Under the big hickory tree on the hill on the other side of the Green Meadows , '' say Spotty .
Then all the Merry Little Breezes clap their hand and shout : `` He do !
He do !
Spotty win the race ! ''
Then they tell how Spotty reach the pond by cling to the tip of Reddy Fox 's tail , and have hide the other two nut , and then how he have patiently crawl home while Billy Mink and Reddy Fox and Peter Rabbit be hunt and hunt and hunt for the nut they could not find .

I BUSTER BEAR GOES FISHING Buster Bear yawn a he lay on his comfortable bed of leaf and watch the first early morning sunbeam creep through the Green Forest to chase out the Black Shadows .
Once more he yawn , and slowly get to his foot and shook himself .
Then he walk over to a big pine-tree , stand up on his hind leg , reach a high up on the trunk of the tree a he could , and scratch the bark with his great claw .
After that he yawn until it seem a if his jaw would crack , and then sit down to think what he want for breakfast .
While he sit there , try to make up his mind what would taste best , he be listen to the sound that tell of the waking of all the little people who live in the Green Forest .
He hear Sammy Jay way off in the distance screaming , `` Thief !
Thief ! ''
and grin .
`` I wonder , '' think Buster , `` if some one have steal Sammy 's breakfast , or if he have steal the breakfast of some one else .
Probably he be the thief himself . ''
He hear Chatterer the Red Squirrel scold as fast a he could make his tongue go and work himself into a terrible rage .
`` Must be that Chatterer get out of bed the wrong way this morning , '' think he .
He hear Blacky the Crow cawing at the top of his lung , and he know by the sound that Blacky be get into mischief of some kind .
He hear the sweet voice of happy little singer , and they be good to hear .
But most of all he listen to a merry , low , silvery laugh that never stop but go on and on , until he just felt a if he must laugh too .
It be the voice of the Laughing Brook .
And a Buster listen it suddenly come to him just what he want for breakfast .
`` I 'm go fishing , '' say he in his deep grumbly-rumbly voice to no one in particular .
`` Yes , Sir , I 'm go fishing .
I want some fat trout for my breakfast . ''
He shuffle along over to the Laughing Brook , and straight to a little pool of which he know , and a he draw near he take the great care not to make the teeny , weeny bit of noise .
Now it just happen that early a he be , some one be before Buster Bear .
When he come in sight of the little pool , who should he see but another fisherman there , who have already catch a fine fat trout .
Who be it ?
Why , Little Joe Otter to be sure .
He be just climb up the bank with the fat trout in his mouth .
Buster Bear 's own mouth water a he saw it .
Little Joe sit down on the bank and prepared to enjoy his breakfast .
He have n't see Buster Bear , and he do n't know that he or any one else be anywhere near .
Buster Bear tiptoe up very softly until he be right behind Little Joe Otter .
`` Woof , woof ! ''
say he in his deepest , most grumbly-rumbly voice .
`` That 's a very fine look trout .
I would n't mind if I have it myself . ''
Little Joe Otter give a frightened squeal and without even turn to see who be speak drop his fish and dive headfirst into the Laughing Brook .
Buster Bear sprang forward and with one of his big paw catch the fat trout just a it be slip back into the water .
`` Here 's your trout , Mr . Otter , '' say he , a Little Joe put his head out of water to see who have frighten him so .
`` Come and get it . ''

II LITTLE JOE OTTER GETS EVEN WITH BUSTER BEAR Little Joe Otter be in a terrible rage .
It be a bad beginning for a beautiful day and Little Joe know it .
But who would n't be in a rage if his breakfast be take from him just a he be about to eat it ?
Anyway , that be what Little Joe tell Billy Mink .
Perhaps he do n't tell it quite exactly a it be , but you know he be very badly frighten at the time .

Of course that be n't nice talk and anything but a nice spirit , but Little Joe Otter 's temper be sometimes pretty short , especially when he be hungry , and this time he have have no breakfast , you know .

Yes , Sir , it be puzzle .

VII FARMER BROWN 'S BOY HAS NO LUCK AT ALL Farmer Brown 's boy tramp through the Green Forest , whistle merrily .

So he whistle a he tramp along , and his whistle be good to hear .
When he reach the first little pool he bait his hook very carefully and then , take the great care to keep out of sight of any trout that might be in the little pool , he begin to fish .
Now Farmer Brown 's boy learn a long time ago that to be a successful fisherman one must have a great deal of patience , so though he do n't get a bite right away a he have expect to , he be n't the least bit discouraged .
He keep very quiet and fished and fish , patiently wait for a foolish trout to take his hook .

There the same thing happen .

Farmer Brown 's boy trudge on to the next pool , and there be a puzzled frown on his freckled face .
Such a thing never have happen before .
He do n't know what to make of it .
All the night before he have dream about the delicious dinner of fry trout he would have the next day , and now -- well , if he do n't catch some trout pretty soon , that splendid dinner would never be anything but a dream .
`` If I do n't know that nobody else come fishing here , I should think that somebody have be here this very morning and caught all the fish or else frighten them so that they be all in hiding , '' say he , a he trudge on to the next little pool .
`` I never have such bad luck in all my life before .
Hello !
What 's this ? ''
There , on the bank beside the little pool , be the head of three trout .
Farmer Brown 's boy scowl down at them more puzzled than ever .
`` Somebody have be fish here , and they have have well luck than I have , '' think he .
He look up the Laughing Brook and down the Laughing Brook and this way and that way , but no one be to be see .
Then he pick up one of the little head and look at it sharply .
`` It be n't cut off with a knife ; it be bite off ! ''
he exclaim .
`` I wonder now if Billy Mink be the scamp who have spoil my fun . ''
Thereafter he keep a sharp lookout for sign of Billy Mink , but though he find two or three more trout head , he saw no other sign and he catch no fish .
This puzzle him more than ever .
It do n't seem possible that such a little fellow a Billy Mink could have catch or frighten all the fish or have eat so many .
Besides , he do n't remember ever have know Billy to leave head around that way .
Billy sometimes catch more fish than he can eat , but then he usually hide them .
The farther he go down the Laughing Brook , the more puzzled Farmer Brown 's boy grow .

VIII FARMER BROWN 'S BOY FEELS HIS HAIR RISE 'T be just a sudden odd surprise Made Farmer Brown 's boy 's hair to rise .
That 's a funny thing for hair to do -- rise up all of a sudden -- be n't it ?
But that be just what the hair on Farmer Brown 's boy 's head do the day he go fish in the Laughing Brook and have no luck at all .
There be just two thing that make hair rise -- anger and fear .
Anger sometimes make the hair on the back and neck of Bowser the Hound and of some other little people bristle and stand up , and you know the hair on the tail of Black Pussy stand on end until her tail look twice as big a it really be .
Both anger and fear make it do that .
But there be only one thing that can make the hair on the head of Farmer Brown 's boy rise , and a it be n't anger , of course it must be fear .
It never have happen before .
You see , there be n't much of anything that Farmer Brown 's boy be really afraid of .
Perhaps he would n't have be afraid this time if it have n't be for the surprise of what he find .
You see when he have find the head of those trout on the bank he know right away that some one else have be fish , and that be why he could n't catch any ; but it do n't seem possible that little Billy Mink could have eat all those trout , and Farmer Brown 's boy do n't once think of Little Joe Otter , and so he be very , very much puzzle .
He be turn it all over in his mind and study what it could mean , when he come to a little muddy place on the bank of the Laughing Brook , and there he saw something that make his eye look a if they would pop right out of his head , and it be right then that he felt his hair rise .

What do you think ?

Now Farmer Brown 's boy do n't know that Buster Bear have come down to the Green Forest to live .

He have a funny feeling , too , that he be be watch , although he could n't see any one .
He be be watch .
Little Joe Otter and Buster Bear be watch him and take the great care to keep out of his sight .

He have n't run , but he have want to .

IX LITTLE JOE OTTER HAS GREAT NEWS TO TELL Little Joe Otter be fairly burst with excitement .

X BUSTER BEAR BECOMES A HERO The news that Little Joe Otter tell at the Smiling Pool , -- how Farmer Brown 's boy have run away from Buster Bear without even see him , -- soon spread all over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest , until every one who live there know about it .

XI BLACKY THE CROW TELLS HIS PLAN Blacky be a dreamer !
Blacky be a schemer !

He want something go on .

XII FARMER BROWN 'S BOY AND BUSTER BEAR GROW CURIOUS Ever since it be light enough to see at all , Blacky the Crow have be sit in the top of the tall tree on the edge of the Green Forest near to Farmer Brown 's house , and never for an instant have he take his eye from Farmer Brown 's back door .

XV BUSTER BEAR IS A FALLEN HERO A fallen hero be some one to whom every one have look up a very brave and then prove to be less brave than he be suppose to be .
That be the way with Buster Bear .
When Little Joe Otter have tell how Farmer Brown 's boy have be afraid at the mere sight of one of Buster Bear 's big footprint , they have at once make a hero of Buster .
At least some of them have .
As this be the first time , the very first time , that they have ever know any one who live in the Green Forest to make Farmer Brown 's boy run away , they look on Buster Bear with a great deal of respect and be very proud of him .
But now they have see Buster Bear and Farmer Brown 's boy meet face to face ; and while it be true that Farmer Brown 's boy have run away as fast a ever he could , it be also true that Buster Bear have do the same thing .
He have run even faster than Farmer Brown 's boy , and have hide in the most lonely place he could find in the very deep part of the Green Forest .
It be hard to believe , but it be true .
And right away everybody lose a great deal of the respect for Buster which they have felt .
It be always that way .
They begin to say unkind thing about him .
They say them among themselves , and some of them even say them to Buster when they meet him , or say them so that he would hear them .
Of course Blacky the Crow and Sammy Jay , who , because they can fly , have nothing to fear from Buster , and who always delight in make other people uncomfortable , never let a chance go by to tell Buster and everybody else within hear what they think of him .
They delight in fly about through the Green Forest until they have find Buster Bear and then from the safety of the tree top scream at him .
`` Buster Bear be big and strong ; His teeth be big ; his claw be long ; In spite of these he run away And hide himself the livelong day ! ''
A dozen time a day Buster would hear them scream this .
He would grind his teeth and glare up at them , but that be all he could do .
He could n't get at them .
He just have to stand it and do nothing .
But when impudent little Chatterer the Red Squirrel shout the same thing from a place just out of reach in a big pine-tree , Buster could stand it no longer .
He give a deep , angry growl that make little shiver run over Chatterer , and then suddenly he start up that tree after Chatterer .
With a frightened little shriek Chatterer scamper to the top of the tree .
He have n't know that Buster could climb .
But Buster be a splendid climber , especially when the tree be big and stout a this one be , and now he go up after Chatterer , growl angrily .
How Chatterer do wish that he have keep his tongue still !
He run to the very top of the tree , so frighten that his teeth chatter , and when he look down and saw Buster 's great mouth come near and nearer , he nearly tumble down with terror .
The bad of it be there be n't another tree near enough for him to jump to .
He be in trouble this time , be Chatterer , sure enough !
And there be no one to help him .
XVI CHATTERER THE RED SQUIRREL JUMPS FOR HIS LIFE It be n't very often that Chatterer the Red Squirrel know fear .
That be one reason that he be so often impudent and saucy .
But once in a while a great fear take possession of him , a when he know that Shadow the Weasel be look for him .
You see , he know that Shadow can go wherever he can go .
There be very few of the little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows who do not know fear at some time or other , but it come to Chatterer as seldom a to any one , because he be very sure of himself and his ability to hide or run away from danger .
But now a he cling to a little branch near the top of a tall pine-tree in the Green Forest and look down at the big sharp teeth of Buster Bear draw nearer and nearer , and listen to the deep , angry growl that make his hair stand on end , Chatterer be too frightened to think .
If only he have keep his tongue still instead of say hateful thing to Buster Bear !
If only he have know that Buster could climb a tree !
If only he have choose a tree near enough to other tree for him to jump across !
But he have say hateful thing , he have choose to sit in a tree which stand quite by itself , and Buster Bear could climb !
Chatterer be in the bad kind of trouble , and there be no one to blame but himself .
That be usually the case with those who get into trouble .
Nearer and nearer come Buster Bear , and deep and angrier sound his voice .
Chatterer give a little frightened gasp and look this way and look that way .
What should he do ?
What could he do !
The ground seem a terrible distance below .
If only he have wing like Sammy Jay !
But he have n't .
`` Gr-r-r-r ! ''
growl Buster Bear .
`` I 'll teach you manner !
I 'll teach you to treat your better with respect !
I 'll swallow you whole , that 's what I 'll do .
Gr-r-r-r ! ''
`` Oh ! ''
cried Chatterer .
`` Gr-r-r-r !
I 'll eat you all up to the last hair on your tail ! ''
growl Buster , scramble a little nearer .
`` Oh !
Oh ! ''
cried Chatterer , and run out to the very tip of the little branch to which he have be cling .
Now if Chatterer have only know it , Buster Bear could n't reach him way up there , because the tree be too small at the top for such a big fellow a Buster .
But Chatterer do n't think of that .
He give one more frightened look down at those big teeth , then he shut his eye and jump -- jump straight out for the far-away ground .
It be a long , long , long way down to the ground , and it certainly look a if such a little fellow a Chatterer must be kill .
But Chatterer have learn from Old Mother Nature that she have give him certain thing to help him at just such time , and one of them be the power to spread himself very flat .
He do it now .
He spread his arm and legs out just as far a he could , and that keep him from fall a fast and as hard a he otherwise would have do , because be spread out so flat that way , the air hold him up a little .
And then there be his tail , that funny little tail he be so fond of jerk when he scold .
This help him too .
It help him keep his balance and keep from turn over and over .
Down , down , down he sail and land on his foot .
Of course , he hit the ground pretty hard , and for just a second he quite lose his breath .
But it be only for a second , and then he be scurry off as fast a a frightened Squirrel could .
Buster Bear watch him and grin .
`` I do n't catch him that time , '' he growl , `` but I guess I give him a good fright and teach him a lesson . ''
XVII BUSTER BEAR GOES BERRYING Buster Bear be a great hand to talk to himself when he think no one be around to overhear .
It 's a habit .
However , it be n't a bad habit unless it be carry too far .
Any habit become bad , if it be carry too far .
Suppose you have a secret , a real secret , something that nobody else know and that you do n't want anybody else to know .
And suppose you have the habit of talk to yourself .
You might , without thinking , you know , tell that secret out loud to yourself , and some one might , just might happen to overhear !
Then there would n't be any secret .
That be the way that a habit which be n't bad in itself can become bad when it be carry too far .
Now Buster Bear have live by himself in the Great Woods so long that this habit of talk to himself have grow and grow .
He do it just to keep from be lonesome .
Of course , when he come down to the Green Forest to live , he bring all his habit with him .
That be one thing about habit , -- you always take them with you wherever you go .
So Buster bring this habit of talk to himself down to the Green Forest , where he have many more neighbor than he have in the Great Woods .
`` Let me see , let me see , what be there to tempt my appetite ? ''
say Buster in his deep , grumbly-rumbly voice .
`` I find my appetite be n't what it ought to be .
I need a change .
Yes , Sir , I need a change .
There be something I ought to have at this time of year , and I have n't get it .
There be something that I use to have and do n't have now .
Ha !
I know !
I need some fresh fruit .
That 's it -- fresh fruit !
It must be about berry time now , and I 'd forget all about it .
My , my , my , how good some berry would taste !
Now if I be back up there in the Great Woods I could have all I could eat .
Um-m-m-m !
Makes my mouth water just to think of it .
There ought to be some up in the Old Pasture .
There ought to be a lot of 'em up there .
If I be n't afraid that some one would see me , I 'd go up there . ''
Buster sigh .
Then he sigh again .
The more he think about those berry he felt sure be grow in the Old Pasture , the more he want some .
It seem to him that never in all his life have he want berry a he do now .
He wander about uneasily .
He be hungry -- hungry for berry and nothing else .
By and by he begin talk to himself again .
`` If I be n't afraid of be see , I 'd go up to the Old Pasture this very minute .
Seems a if I could taste those berry . ''
He lick his lip hungrily a he speak .
Then his face brighten .
`` I know what I 'll do !
I 'll go up there at the very first peep of day to-morrow .
I can eat all I want and get back to the Green Forest before there be any danger that Farmer Brown 's boy or any one else I 'm afraid of will see me .
That 's just what I 'll do .
My , I wish to-morrow morning would hurry up and come . ''
Now though Buster do n't know it , some one have be listen , and that some one be none other than Sammy Jay .
When at last Buster lay down for a nap , Sammy fly away , chuckle to himself .
`` I believe I 'll visit the Old Pasture to-morrow morning myself , '' think he .
`` I have an idea that something interesting may happen if Buster do n't change his mind . ''
Sammy be on the lookout very early the next morning .
The first Jolly Little Sunbeams have only reach the Green Meadows and have not start to creep into the Green Forest , when he saw a big , dark form steal out of the Green Forest where it join the Old Pasture .
It move very swiftly and silently , a if in a great hurry .
Sammy know who it be : it be Buster Bear , and he be go berrying .
Sammy wait a little until he could see good .
Then he too start for the Old Pasture .
XVIII SOMEBODY ELSE GOES BERRYING Is n't it funny how two people will often think of the same thing at the same time , and neither one know that the other be think of it ?
That be just what happen the day that Buster Bear first think of go berrying .
While he be walk around in the Green Forest , talk to himself about how hungry he be for some berry and how sure he be that there must be some up in the Old Pasture , some one else be think about berry and about the Old Pasture too .
`` Will you make me a berry pie if I will get the berry to-morrow ? ''
ask Farmer Brown 's boy of his mother .
Of course Mrs. Brown promise that she would , and so that night Farmer Brown 's boy go to bed very early that he might get up early in the morning , and all night long he dream of berry and berry pie .
He be awake even before jolly , round , red Mr. Sun think it be time to get up , and he be all ready to start for the Old Pasture when the first Jolly Little Sunbeams come dance across the Green Meadows .
He carry a big tin pail , and in the bottom of it , wrap up in a piece of paper , be a lunch , for he mean to stay until he fill that pail , if it take all day .
Now the Old Pasture be very large .
It lie at the foot of the Big Mountain , and even extend a little way up on the Big Mountain .
There be room in it for many people to pick berry all day without even see each other , unless they roam about a great deal .
You see , the bush grow very thick there , and you can not see very far in any direction .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun have climb a little way up in the sky by the time Farmer Brown 's boy reach the Old Pasture , and be smile down on all the Great World , and all the Great World seem to be smile back .
Farmer Brown 's boy start to whistle , and then he stop .
`` If I whistle , '' think he , `` everybody will know just where I be , and will keep out of sight , and I never can get acquaint with folk if they keep out of sight . ''
You see , Farmer Brown 's boy be just begin to understand something that Peter Rabbit and the other little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest learn almost as soon a they learn to walk , -- that if you do n't want to be see , you must n't be hear .
So he do n't whistle a he felt like do , and he try not to make a bit of noise a he follow an old cow-path towards a place where he know the berry grow thick and oh , so big , and all the time he keep his eye wide open , and he keep his ear open too .
That be how he happen to hear a little cry , a very faint little cry .
If he have be whistle , he would n't have hear it at all .
He stop to listen .
He never have hear a cry just like it before .
At first he could n't make out just what it be or where it come from .
But one thing he be sure of , and that be that it be a cry of fright .
He stand perfectly still and listen with all his might .
There it be again -- `` Help !
Help !
Help '' -- and it be very faint and sound terribly frighten .
He wait a minute or two , but hear nothing more .
Then he put down his pail and begin a hurried look here , there , and everywhere .
He be sure that it have come from somewhere on the ground , so he peer behind bush and peep behind log and stone , and then just a he have about give up hope of find where it come from , he go around a little turn in the old cow-path , and there right in front of him be little Mr. Gartersnake , and what do you think he be do ?
Well , I do n't like to tell you , but he be try to swallow one of the child of Stickytoes the Tree Toad .
Of course Farmer Brown 's Boy do n't let him .
He make little Mr. Gartersnake set Master Stickytoes free and hold Mr. Gartersnake until Master Stickytoes be safely out of reach .
XIX BUSTER BEAR HAS A FINE TIME Buster Bear be have the fine time he have have since he come down from the Great Woods to live in the Green Forest .
To be sure , he be n't in the Green Forest now , but he be n't far from it .
He be in the Old Pasture , one edge of which touch one edge of the Green Forest .
And where do you think he be , in the Old Pasture ?
Why , right in the middle of the big patch of the big blueberry he ever have see in all his life !
Now if there be any one thing that Buster Bear have rather have above another , it be all the berry he can eat , unless it be honey .
Nothing can quite equal honey in Buster 's mind .
But next to honey give him berry .
He be n't particular what kind of berry .
Raspberries , blackberry , or blueberry , either kind , will make him perfectly happy .
`` Um-m-m , my , my , but these be good ! ''
he mumble in his deep grumbly-rumbly voice , a he sit on his haunch strip off the berry greedily .
His little eye twinkle with enjoyment , and he do n't mind at all if now and then he get leaf , and some green berry in his mouth with the big ripe berry .
He do n't try to get them out .
Oh , my , no !
He just chomp them all up together and pat his stomach from sheer delight .
Now Buster have reach the Old Pasture just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun have creep out of bed , and he have fully make up his mind that he would be back in the Green Forest before Mr. Sun have climb very far up in the blue , blue sky .
You see , big a he be and strong a he be , Buster Bear be very shy and bashful , and he have no desire to meet Farmer Brown , or Farmer Brown 's boy , or any other of those two-legged creature call men .
It seem funny but he actually be afraid of them .
And he have a feeling that he be a great deal more likely to meet one of them in the Old Pasture than deep in the Green Forest .
So when he start to look for berry , he make up his mind that he would eat what he could in a great hurry and get back to the Green Forest before Farmer Brown 's boy be more than out of bed .
But when he find those berry he be so hungry that he forget his fear and everything else .
They taste so good that he just have to eat and eat and eat .
Now you know that Buster be a very big fellow , and it take a lot to fill him up .
He keep eat and eat and eating , and the more he eat the more he want .
You know how it be .
So he wander from one patch of berry to another in the Old Pasture , and never once think of the time .
Somehow , time be the hard thing in the world to remember , when you be have a good time .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun climb high and higher in the blue , blue sky .
He look down on all the Great World and saw all that be go on .
He saw Buster Bear in the Old Pasture , and smile a he saw what a perfectly glorious time Buster be have .
And he saw something else in the Old Pasture that make his smile still broad .
He saw Farmer Brown 's boy fill a great tin pail with blueberry , and he know that Farmer Brown 's boy do n't know that Buster Bear be anywhere about , and he know that Buster Bear do n't know that Farmer Brown 's boy be anywhere about , and somehow he felt very sure that he would see something funny happen if they should chance to meet .
`` Um-m-m , um-m-m , '' mumble Buster Bear with his mouth full , a he move along to another patch of berry .
And then he give a little gasp of surprise and delight .
Right in front of him be a shiny thing just full of the fine , big , blue berry !
There be no leaf or green one there .
Buster blink his greedy little eye rapidly and look again .
No , he be n't dream .
They be real berry , and all he have get to do be to help himself .
Buster look sharply at the shiny thing that hold the berry .
It seem perfectly harmless .
He reach out a big paw and push it gently .
It tip over and spill out a lot of the berry .
Yes , it be perfectly harmless .
Buster give a little sigh of pure happiness .
He would eat those berry to the last one , and then he would go home to the Green Forest .
XX BUSTER BEAR CARRIES OFF THE PAIL OF FARMER BROWN 'S BOY The question be , do Buster Bear steal Farmer Brown 's boy 's pail ?
To steal be to take something which belong to some one else .
There be no doubt that he steal the berry that be in the pail when he find it , for he deliberately eat them .
He know well enough that some one must have pick them -- for whoever heard of blueberry grow in tin pail ?
So there be no doubt that when Buster take them , he steal them .
But with the pail it be different .
He take the pail , but he do n't mean to take it .
In fact , he do n't want that pail at all .
You see it be this way : When Buster find that big tin pail brim full of delicious berry in the shade of that big bush in the Old Pasture , he do n't stop to think whether or not he have a right to them .
Buster be so fond of berry that from the very second that his greedy little eye saw that pailful , he forget everything but the feast that be wait for him right under his very nose .
He do n't think anything about the right or wrong of help himself .
There before him be more berry than he have ever see together at one time in all his life , and all he have to do be to eat and eat and eat .
And that be just what he do do .
Of course he upset the pail , but he do n't mind a little thing like that .
When he have gobble up all the berry that roll out , he thrust his nose into the pail to get all that be leave in it .
Just then he hear a little noise , a if some one be come .
He throw up his head to listen , and somehow , he never do know just how , the handle of the pail slip back over his ear and caught there .
This be bad enough , but to make matter bad , just at that very minute he hear a shrill , angry voice shout , `` Hi , there !
Get out of there ! ''
He do n't need to be tell whose voice that be .
It be the voice of Farmer Brown 's boy .
Right then and there Buster Bear nearly have a fit .
There be that awful pail fast over his head so that he could n't see a thing .
Of course , that mean that he could n't run away , which be the thing of all thing he most want to do , for big a he be and strong a he be , Buster be very shy and bashful when human being be around .
He growl and whine and squeal .
He try to back out of the pail and could n't .
He try to shake it off and could n't .
He try to pull it off , but somehow he could n't get hold of it .
Then there be another yell .
If Buster have n't be so frightened himself , he might have recognize that second yell a one of fright , for that be what it be .
You see Farmer Brown 's boy have just discover Buster Bear .
When he have yell the first time , he have suppose that it be one of the young cattle who live in the Old Pasture all summer , but when he saw Buster , he be just as badly frighten a Buster himself .
In fact , he be too surprised and frighten even to run .
After that second yell he just stand still and star .
Buster claw at that awful thing on his head more frantically than ever .
Suddenly it slip off , so that he could see .
He give one frightened look at Farmer Brown 's boy , and then with a mighty `` Woof ! ''
he start for the Green Forest as fast a his leg could take him , and this be very fast indeed , let me tell you .
He do n't stop to pick out a path , but just crash through the bush a if they be nothing at all , just nothing at all .
But the funny thing of all be this -- he take that pail with him !
Yes , Sir , Buster Bear run away with the big tin pail of Farmer Brown 's boy !
You see when it slip off his head , the handle be still around his neck , and there he be run away with a pail hang from his neck !
He do n't want it .
He would have give anything to get rid of it .
But he take it because he could n't help it .
And that bring u back to the question , do Buster steal Farmer Brown 's boy 's pail ?
What do you think ?
XXI SAMMY JAY MAKES THINGS WORSE FOR BUSTER BEAR `` Thief , thief , thief !
Thief , thief , thief ! ''
Sammy Jay be scream at the top of his lung , a he follow Buster Bear across the Old Pasture towards the Green Forest .
Never have he scream so loud , and never have his voice sound so excited .
The little people of the Green Forest , the Green Meadows , and the Smiling Pool be so used to hear Sammy cry thief that usually they think very little about it .
But every bless one who hear Sammy this morning stop whatever he be do and prick up his ear to listen .
Sammy 's cousin , Blacky the Crow , just happen to be fly along the edge of the Old Pasture , and the minute he hear Sammy 's voice , he turn and fly over to see what it be all about .
Just as soon a he catch sight of Buster Bear run for the Green Forest as hard a ever he could , he understand what have excite Sammy so .
He be so surprised that he almost forget to keep his wing move .
Buster Bear have what look to Blacky very much like a tin pail hang from his neck !
No wonder Sammy be excite .
Blacky beat his wing fiercely and start after Sammy .
And so they reach the edge of the Green Forest , Buster Bear run as hard a ever he could , Sammy Jay fly just behind him and screaming , `` Thief , thief , thief ! ''
at the top of his lung , and behind him Blacky the Crow , try to catch up and yell as loud a he could , `` Caw , caw , caw !
Come on , everybody !
Come on !
Come on ! ''
Poor Buster !
It be bad enough to be frighten almost to death a he have be up in the Old Pasture when the pail have catch over his head just a Farmer Brown 's boy have yell at him .
Then to have the handle of the pail slip down around his neck so that he could n't get rid of the pail but have to take it with him a he run , be make a bad matter worse .
Now to have all his neighbor of the Green Forest see him in such a fix and make fun of him , be more than he could stand .
He felt humiliate .
That be just another way of say sham .
Yes , Sir , Buster felt that he be sham in the eye of his neighbor , and he want nothing so much a to get away by himself , where no one could see him , and try to get rid of that dreadful pail .
But Buster be so big that it be not easy for him to find a hiding place .
So , when he reach the Green Forest , he keep right on to the deepest , dark , most lonesome part and crept under the thick hemlock-tree he could find .
But it be of no use .
The sharp eye of Sammy Jay and Blacky the Crow saw him .
They actually fly into the very tree under which he be hide , and how they do scream !
Pretty soon Ol ' Mistah Buzzard come drop down out of the blue , blue sky and take a seat on a convenient dead tree , where he could see all that go on .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard begin to grin as soon a he saw that tin pail on Buster 's neck .
Then come others , -- Redtail the Hawk , Scrapper the Kingbird , Redwing the Blackbird , Drummer the Woodpecker , Welcome Robin , Tommy Tit the Chickadee , Jenny Wren , Redeye the Vireo , and ever so many more .
They come from the Old Orchard , the Green Meadows , and even down by the Smiling Pool , for the voice of Sammy Jay and Blacky the Crow carry far , and at the sound of them everybody hurry over , sure that something exciting be go on .
Presently Buster hear light footstep , and peep out , he saw Billy Mink and Peter Rabbit and Jumper the Hare and Prickly Porky and Reddy Fox and Jimmy Skunk .
Even timid little Whitefoot the Wood Mouse be where he could peer out and see without be see .
Of course , Chatterer the Red Squirrel and Happy Jack the Gray Squirrel be there .
There they all sit in a great circle around him , each where he felt safe , but where he could see , and every one of them laugh and make fun of Buster .
`` Thief , thief , thief ! ''
scream Sammy until his throat be sore .
The bad of it be Buster know that everybody know that it be true .
That awful pail be proof of it .
`` I wish I never have think of berry , '' growl Buster to himself .
XXII BUSTER BEAR HAS A FIT OF TEMPER A temper be a bad , bad thing When once it get away .
There 's nothing quite at all like it To spoil a pleasant day .
Buster Bear be in a terrible temper .
Yes , Sir , Buster Bear be have the bad fit of temper ever see in the Green Forest .
And the bad part of it all be that all his neighbor of the Green Forest and a whole lot from the Green Meadows and the Smiling Pool be also there to see it .
It be bad enough to give way to temper when you be all alone , and there be no one to watch you , but when you let temper get the best of you right where others see you , oh , dear , dear , it certainly be a sorry sight .
Now ordinarily Buster be one of the most good-natured person in the world .
It take a great deal to rouse his temper .
He be n't one tenth so quick temper a Chatterer the Red Squirrel , or Sammy Jay , or Reddy Fox .
But when his temper be arouse and get away from him , then watch out !
It seem to Buster that he have have all that he could stand that day and a little more .
First have come the fright back there in the Old Pasture .
Then the pail have slip down behind his ear and hold fast , so he have run all the way to the Green Forest with it hang about his neck .
This be bad enough , for he know just how funny he must look , and besides , it be very uncomfortable .
But to have Sammy Jay call everybody within hear to come and see him be more than he could stand .
It seem to Buster a if everybody who live in the Green Forest , on the Green Meadows , or around the Smiling Brook , be sit around his hiding place , laugh and make fun of him .
It be more than any self-respecting Bear could stand .
With a roar of anger Buster Bear charge out of his hide place .
He rush this way and that way !
He roar with all his might !
He be very terrible to see .
Those who could fly , flew .
Those who could climb , climb .
And those who be swift of foot , ran .
A few who could neither fly nor climb nor run fast , hid and lay shaking and tremble for fear that Buster would find them .
In less time than it take to tell about it , Buster be alone .
At least , he could n't see any one .
-LSB- Illustration : Those who could fly , flew .
Those who could climb , climb .
Page 112 .
-RSB- Then he vent his temper on the tin pail .
He cuff at it and pull at it , all the time growl angrily .
He lay down and claw at it with his hind foot .
At last the handle broke , and he be free !
He shake himself .
Then he jump on the helpless pail .
With a blow of a big paw he send it clatter against a tree .
He try to bite it .
Then he once more fell to knock it this way and that way , until it be pound flat , and no one would ever have guess that it have once be a pail .
Then , and not till then , do Buster recover his usual good nature .
Little by little , a he think it all over , a look of shame crept into his face .
`` I -- I guess it be n't the fault of that thing .
I ought to have know enough to keep my head out of it , '' he say slowly and thoughtfully .
`` You get no more than you deserve for steal Farmer Brown 's boy 's berry , '' say Sammy Jay , who have come back and be look on from the top of a tree .
`` You ought to know by this time that no good come of steal . ''
Buster Bear look up and grin , and there be a twinkle in his eye .
`` You ought to know , Sammy Jay , '' say he .
`` I hope you 'll always remember it . ''
`` Thief , thief , thief ! ''
scream Sammy , and fly away .
XXIII FARMER BROWN 'S BOY LUNCHES ON BERRIES When thing go wrong in spite of you To smile 's the best thing you can do -- To smile and say , `` I 'm mighty glad They be no bad ; they 're not so bad ! ''
That be what Farmer Brown 's boy say when he find that Buster Bear have steal the berry he have work so hard to pick and then have run off with the pail .
You see , Farmer Brown 's boy be learn to be something of a philosopher , one of those people who accept bad thing cheerfully and right away see how they be good than they might have be .
When he have first heard some one in the bush where he have hide his pail of berry , he have be very sure that it be one of the cow or young cattle who live in the Old Pasture during the summer .
He have be afraid that they might stupidly kick over the pail and spill the berry , and he have hurry to drive whoever it be away .
It have n't enter his head that it could be anybody who would eat those berry .
When he have yell and Buster Bear have suddenly appear , struggle to get off the pail which have catch over his head , Farmer Brown 's boy have be too frighten to even move .
Then he have see Buster tear away through the brush even more frightened than he be , and right away his courage have begin to come back .
`` If he be so afraid of me , I guess I need n't be afraid of him , '' say he .
`` I 've lose my berry , but it be worth it to find out that he be afraid of me .
There be plenty more on the bush , and all I 've get to do be to pick them .
It might be bad . ''
He walk over to the place where the pail have be , and then he remember that when Buster run away he have carry the pail with him , hang about his neck .
He whistle .
It be a comical little whistle of chagrin a he realize that he have nothing in which to put more berry , even if he pick them .
`` It 's bad than I think , '' cry he .
`` That bear have cheat me out of that berry pie my mother promise me . ''
Then he begin to laugh , a he think of how funny Buster Bear have look with the pail about his neck , and then because , you know he be learn to be a philosopher , he once more repeated , `` It might have be bad .
Yes , indeed , it might have be bad .
That bear might have try to eat me instead of the berry .
I guess I 'll go eat that lunch I leave back by the spring , and then I 'll go home .
I can pick berry some other day . ''
Chuckling happily over Buster Bear 's great fright , Farmer Brown 's boy tramp back to the spring where he have leave two thick sandwich on a flat stone when he start to save his pail of berry .
`` My , but those sandwich will taste good , '' think he .
`` I 'm glad they be big and thick .
I never be hungrier in my life .
Hello ! ''
This he exclaim right out loud , for he have just come in sight of the flat stone where the sandwich should have be , and they be not there .
No , Sir , there be n't so much a a crumb left of those two thick sandwich .
You see , Old Man Coyote have find them and gobble them up while Farmer Brown 's boy be away .
But Farmer Brown 's boy do n't know anything about Old Man Coyote .
He rub his eye and star everywhere , even up in the tree , a if he think those sandwich might be hang up there .
They have disappear as completely a if they never have be , and Old Man Coyote have take care to leave no trace of his visit .
Farmer Brown 's boy gap foolishly this way and that way .
Then , instead of grow angry , a slow smile stole over his freckled face .
`` I guess some one else be hungry too , '' he mutter .
`` Wonder who it be ?
Guess this Old Pasture be no place for me to-day .
I 'll fill up on berry and then I 'll go home . ''
So Farmer Brown 's boy make his lunch on blueberry and then rather sheepishly he start for home to tell of all the strange thing that have happen to him in the Old Pasture .
Two or three time , a he trudge along , he stop to scratch his head thoughtfully .
`` I guess , '' say he at last , `` that I 'm not so smart a I think I be , and I 've get a lot to learn yet . ''
This be the end of the adventure of Buster Bear in this book because -- guess why .
Because Old Mr. Toad insist that I must write a book about his adventure , and Old Mr. Toad be such a good friend of all of u that I be go to do it .

I CHATTERER THE RED SQUIRREL RUNS FOR HIS LIFE Chatterer the Red Squirrel have be scold because there be no excitement .
He have even try to make some excitement by wake Bobby Coon and make him so angry that Bobby have threaten to eat him alive .
It have be great fun to dance around and call Bobby name and make fun of him .
Oh , yes , it have be great fun .
You see , he know all the time that Bobby could n't catch him if he should try .
But now thing be different .
Chatterer have all the excitement that he want .
Indeed , he have more than he want .
The truth be , Chatterer be run for his life , and he know it .
It be a terrible thing , a very terrible thing to have to run for one 's life .
Peter Rabbit know all about it .
He have run for his life often .
Sometimes it have be Reddy Fox behind him , sometimes Bowser the Hound , and once or twice Old Man Coyote .
Peter have know that on his long legs his life have depend , and more than once a terrible fear have fill his heart .
But Peter have also know that if he could reach the old stone wall or the dear Old Briar-patch first , he would be safe , and he always have reach it .
So when he have be run with that terrible fear in his heart , there have always be hope there , too .
But Chatterer the Red Squirrel be run without hope .
Yes , Sir , there be nothing but fear , terrible fear , in his heart , for he know not where to go .
The hollow tree or the hole in the old stone wall where he would be safe from any one else , even Farmer Brown 's boy , offer him no safety now , for the one who be follow him with hunger in his anger-red eye could go anywhere that he could go -- could go into any hole big enough for him to squeeze into .
You see , it be Shadow the Weasel from whom Chatterer be run , and Shadow be so slim that he can slip in and out of place that even Chatterer can not get through .
Chatterer know all this , and so , because it be of no use to run to his usual safe hiding place , he run in just the other direction .
He do n't know where he be go .
He have just one thought : to run and run as long a he could and then , well , he would try to fight , though he know it would be of no use .
`` Oh , dear !
Oh , dear ! ''
he sob , a he run out on the branch of a tree and leap across to the next tree , `` I wish I have mind my own business !
I wish I have keep my tongue still .
Shadow the Weasel would n't have know where I be if he have n't hear my voice .
Oh , dear !
oh , dear me !
What can I do ?
What can I do ? ''
Now in his great fright Chatterer have run and jump so hard that he be begin to grow very tired .
Presently he find that he must make a very long jump to reach the next tree .
He have often make a long a jump a this and think nothing of it , but now he be so tired that the distance look twice as great a it really be .
He do n't dare stop to run down the tree and scamper across .
So he take a long breath , run swiftly along the branch , and leap .
His hand just touch the tip of the near branch of the other tree .
He try his very best to hold on , but he could n't .
Then down , down , down he fell .
He spread himself out as flat a he could , and that save him a little , but still it be a dreadful fall , and when he land , it seem for just a minute a if all the breath be go from his body .
But it be n't quite , and in another minute he be scramble up the tree .
II CHATTERER 'S LAST CHANCE Chatterer , still run for his life and without the least hope , suddenly saw a last chance to escape from Shadow the Weasel .
That be , he saw something that might offer him a chance .
He could n't be sure until he have try , and even then he might escape from one danger only to run right into another equally great .
What Chatterer saw be a big brown bunch near the top of a tall chestnut-tree , and he head for that tree as fast a ever he could go .
What be that big brown bunch ?
Why it be Redtail the Hawk , who be doze there with his head draw down between his shoulder dream .
Now old Redtail be one of Chatterer 's deadly enemy .
He be quite a fond of Red Squirrel a be Shadow the Weasel , though he do n't often try to catch one , because there be other thing to eat much easy to get .
Chatterer have have more than one narrow escape from old Redtail and be very much afraid of him , yet here he be run up the very tree in which Redtail be sit .
You see , a very daring idea have come into his head .
He have see at once that Redtail be doze and have n't see him at all .
He know that Redtail would just as soon have Shadow the Weasel for dinner a himself , and a very daring plan have pop into his head .
`` I may as well be catch by Redtail a Shadow , '' he think , a he run up the tree , `` but if my plan work out right , I wo n't be catch by either .
Anyway , it be my very last chance . ''
Up the tree he scramble , and after him go Shadow the Weasel .
Shadow have be so intent on catch Chatterer that he have not notice old Redtail , which be just a Chatterer have hop .
Up , up he scramble , straight past old Redtail , but a he pass , he pull one of Redtail 's long tail feather , and then run on to the top of the tree , and with the last bit of strength he have leave , leap to a neighboring spruce-tree where , hide by the thick branch , he stop to rest and see what would happen .
Of course , when he felt his tail pull , old Redtail be wide awake in a flash ; and of course he look down to see who have dare to pull his tail .
There just below him be Shadow the Weasel , who have just that minute discover who be sit there .
Old Redtail hiss sharply , and the feather on the top of his head stand up in a way they do when he be angry .
And he be angry -- very angry .
Shadow the Weasel stop short .
Then , like a flash , he dodge around to the other side of the tree .
He have no thought of Chatterer now .
Things be change all in an instant , quite change .
Instead of the hunter , he be now the hunt .
Old Redtail circle in the air just overhead , and every time he catch sight of Shadow , he swoop at him with great , cruel claw spread to clutch him .
Shadow dodge around the trunk of the tree .
He be more angry than frighten , for his sharp eye have spy a little hollow in a branch of the chestnut-tree , and he know that once inside of that , he would have nothing to fear .
But he be angry clear through to think that he should be cheat out of that dinner he have be so sure of only a few minute before .
So he screech angrily at old Redtail and then , watch his chance , scamper out to the hollow and whisk inside , just in the nick of time .
Chatterer , watch from the spruce-tree , give a great sigh of relief .
He saw Redtail the Hawk post himself on the top of a tall tree where he could keep watch of that hollow in which Shadow have disappear , and he know that it would be a long time before Shadow would dare poke even his nose outside .
Then , as soon a he be rest , Chatterer steal softly , oh , so softly , away through the tree-tops until he be sure that Redtail could not see him .
Then he hurry .
He want to get just a far away from Shadow the Weasel a he could .
III CHATTERER TELLS SAMMY JAY ABOUT SHADOW THE WEASEL Chatterer hurry through the Green Forest .
He do n't know just where he be go .
He have but one thought , and that be to get a far away from Shadow the Weasel a he could .
It make him have cold shiver all over every time he think of Shadow .
`` Seems to me you be in a great hurry , '' say a voice from a pine-tree he be pass .
Chatterer know that voice without look to see who be speak .
Everybody in the Green Forest know that voice .
It be the voice of Sammy Jay .
`` It look to me a if you be run away from some one , '' jeer Sammy .
Chatterer want to stop and pick a quarrel with Sammy , a he usually do when they meet , but the fear of Shadow the Weasel be still upon him .
`` I -- I -- be , '' he say in a very low voice .
Sammy look a if he think he have n't hear right .
Never before have he know Chatterer to admit that he be afraid , for you know Chatterer be a great boaster .
It must be something very serious to frighten Chatterer like that .
`` What 's that ? ''
Sammy ask sharply .
`` I always know you to be a coward , but this be the first time I have ever know you to admit it .
Who be you run away from ? ''
Illustration : `` What 's that ? ''
Sammy ask sharply .
`` Shadow the Weasel , '' reply Chatterer , still in a very low voice , a if he be afraid of be overheard .
`` Shadow the Weasel be back in the Green Forest , and I have just have such a narrow escape ! ''
`` Ho ! ''
cry Sammy , `` this be important .
I think Shadow be up in the Old Pasture .
If he have come back to the Green Forest , folk ought to know it .
Where be he now ? ''
Chatterer stop and tell Sammy all about his narrow escape and how he have leave Shadow the Weasel in a hollow of a chestnut-tree with Redtail the Hawk watching for him to come out .
Sammy 's eye sparkle when Chatterer tell how he have pull the tail of old Redtail .
`` And he do n't know now who do it ; he think it be Shadow , '' conclude Chatterer , with a weak little grin .
`` Ho , ho , ho !
Ha , ha , ha ! ''
laugh Sammy Jay .
`` I wish I have be there to see it . ''
Then he suddenly grow grave .
`` Other folk certainly ought to know that Shadow be back in the Green Forest , '' say he , `` so that they may be on their guard .
Then if they get catch , it be their own fault .
I think I 'll go spread the news . ''
You see , for all his mean way , Sammy Jay do have some good in him , just a everybody do , and he dearly love to tell important news .
`` I -- I wish you would go first of all and tell my cousin , Happy Jack the Gray Squirrel , '' say Chatterer , speaking in a hesitating way .
Sammy Jay lean over and look at Chatterer sharply .
`` I think you and Happy Jack be not friend , '' say he .
`` You always seem to be quarrel . ''
Chatterer look a little confused , but he be very quick with his tongue , be Chatterer .
`` That 's just it , '' he reply quickly .
`` That 's just it !
If anything should happen to Happy Jack , I would n't have him to quarrel with , and it be such fun to see him get mad ! ''
Now of course the real reason why Chatterer want Happy Jack warn be because down inside he be ashamed of a dreadful thought that have come to him of lead Shadow the Weasel to Happy Jack 's house , so that he himself might escape .
It have be a dreadful thought , a cowardly think , and Chatterer have be really ashamed that he should have ever have such a thought .
He think now that if he could do something for Happy Jack , he would feel well about it .
Sammy Jay promise to go straight to Happy Jack and warn him that Shadow the Weasel be back in the Green Forest , and off he start , scream the news a he fly , so that all the little people in the Green Forest might know .
Chatterer listen a few minute and then start on .
`` Where shall I go ? ''
he mutter .
`` Where shall I go ?
I do n't dare stay in the Green Forest , for now Shadow will never rest until he catch me . ''
IV CHATTERER LEAVES THE GREEN FOREST Chatterer be in a peck of trouble .
Yes , Sir , he be in a peck of trouble .
There be no doubt about it .
`` Oh , dear !
Oh , dear !
If only I have keep my tongue still !
If only I have keep my tongue still ! ''
he keep say over and over to himself , a he hurry through the Green Forest .
You see , Chatterer be just begin to realize what a lot of trouble an unruly tongue can get one into .
Here it be cold weather , the very edge of winter , and Chatterer do n't dare stay in the Green Forest where he have always make his home .
His storehouse be full of nut and seed and corn , enough and more than enough to keep him in comfort all winter , and now he must turn his back on them and go he do n't know where , and all because of his mean disposition and bad tongue .
If he have n't call Bobby Coon name that morning at the top of his voice , Shadow the Weasel might not have find him .
He know that Shadow have a long memory , and that he would never forget the trick by which Chatterer have escape , and so the only way Chatterer would ever be able to have a moment 's peace would be to leave the Green Forest for as long a Shadow the Weasel choose to stay there .
Chatterer shiver inside his warm , red fur coat a he think of the long , cold winter and how hard it would be to find enough to eat .
Was ever any one else in such a dreadful fix ?
Presently he come to the edge of the Green Forest .
He sit down to rest in the top of a tree where he could look off over the Green Meadows .
Far , far away he could see the Purple Hills , behind which jolly , round , red Mr. Sun go to bed every night .
He could see the old stone wall that separate Farmer Brown 's cornfield from the Green Meadows .
He could see Farmer Brown 's house and barn and near them the Old Orchard where Johnny Chuck have spend the summer with Polly Chuck and their baby Chucks .
He know every nook and corner in the old stone wall and many time he have be to the Old Orchard .
It be there that he have steal the egg of Drummer the Woodpecker .
He grin at the thought of those egg and how he have steal them , and then he shiver a he remember how he have finally be catch and how sharp the bill of Drummer and Mrs. Drummer be .
But all that be in the past , and think about it be n't go to help him now .
He have get to do something right away .
Perhaps he might find a place to live in the old stone wall , and there might , there just might , be enough grain of corn scatter over the ground of the cornfield for him to lay up a supply , if he work very hard and fast .
Anyway , he would have a look .
So he hurry down from the tree and out along the old stone wall .
His spirit begin to rise a he whisk along , peer into every hole and jumping from stone to stone .
It really seem a though he might find a snug home somewhere here .
Then he remember something that make his heart sink again .
He remember have see Shadow the Weasel more than once explore that very wall .
Just as likely a not he would do it again , for it be so very near the Green Forest .
No , the old stone wall would n't do .
Just then along come Peter Rabbit .
Peter saw right away that something be wrong with Chatterer , and he want to know what it be .
Chatterer tell him .
He felt that he have just get to tell some one .
Peter look thoughtful .
He scratch his long left ear with his long right hind foot .
`` You know there be another old stone wall up there by the Old Orchard , '' say he .
`` It be pretty near Farmer Brown 's house , and Black Pussy hunt there a great deal , but you ought to be smart enough to keep out of her clutch . ''
`` I should hope so ! ''
exclaim Chatterer scornfully .
`` I have never see a cat yet that I be afraid of !
believe I 'll go over and have a look at that old wall , Peter Rabbit . ''
`` I 'll go with you , '' say Peter , and off they start together .
V CHATTERER FINDS A HOME When your plan be upset and all scatter about Just make up your mind that you 'll find a way out .
Peter rabbit go straight over to the old stone wall on the edge of the Old Orchard , lipperty-lipperty-lip so fast that it do n't take him long to get there .
But Chatterer the Red Squirrel never feel really safe on the ground unless there be something to climb close at hand , so he go a long way round by way of the rail fence .
He always do like to run along a rail fence , and he would n't have mind it a bit this morning if he have n't be in such a hurry .
It seem to him that he never would get there .
But of course he do .
When he do get there , he find Peter Rabbit sit on Johnny Chuck 's doorstep , star down Johnny Chuck 's long hall .
`` They 're asleep , '' say he , a Chatterer come up all out of breath .
`` I 've thump and thump and thump , but it be n't the least bit of use .
They be asleep , and they 'll stay asleep until Mistress Spring arrive .
I ca n't understand it at all .
No , Sir , I ca n't understand how anybody can be willing to miss this splendid cold weather . ''
Peter shake his head in a puzzled way and continue to stare down the long empty hall .
Of course he be talk about Johnny and Polly Chuck , who have go to sleep for the winter .
That sleep business always puzzle Peter .
It seem to him like a terrible waste of time .
But Chatterer have too much on his mind to waste time wonder how other people could sleep all winter .
He could n't himself , and now that he have be drive away from his own home in the Green Forest by fear of Shadow the Weasel , he could n't waste a minute .
He must find a new home and then spend every minute of daytime lay up a new store of food for the day when everything would be cover with snow .
Up and down the length of the stone wall he scamper , look for a place to make a home , but nothing suit him .
You know he like best to make his home in a tree .
He be n't like Striped Chipmunk , who live in the ground .
Poor Chatterer !
He just could n't see how he be go to live in the old stone wall .
He sit on top of a big stone to rest and think it over .
He be discourage .
Life do n't seem worth the living just then .
He felt a if his heart have go way down to his toe .
Just then his eye saw something that make his heart come up again with a great bound right where it ought to be , and just then Peter Rabbit come hop along .
`` Have you find a new home yet ? ''
ask Peter .
`` Yes , '' reply Chatterer , `` I think I have .
`` That 's good , '' reply Peter .
`` I be sure you would find one over here .
Where be it ? ''
Illustration : `` Have you find a new home yet ? ''
ask Peter .
Chatterer open his mouth to tell Peter and then close it with a snap .
He remember just in time how hard it be for Peter to keep a secret .
If he should tell Peter , it would be just like Peter to tell some one else without mean to , and then it might get back to Shadow the Weasel .
`` I 'm not go to tell you now , Peter Rabbit , '' say he .
`` You see , I do n't want anybody to know where it be until I be sure that it will do .

VI PETER RABBIT LISTENS TO THE WRONG VOICE Peter Rabbit do n't play fair .
No , Sir , Peter do n't play fair .
People who have too much curiosity about other people 's affair seldom do play fair .
He do n't mean to be unfair .
Oh , my , no !
Peter do n't mean to be unfair .
When he leave Chatterer the Red Squirrel sit on the old stone wall on the edge of Farmer Brown 's Old Orchard , he intend to go straight home to the dear Old Briar-patch .
He be a little disappointed , be Peter , that Chatterer have n't tell him just where his new house be .
Not that it really matter ; he just want to know , that be all .
With every jump away from the old stone wall , that desire to know just where Chatterer 's new house be seem to grow .
Peter stop and look back .
He could n't see Chatterer now , because the bush hide him .
And if he could n't see Chatterer , why of course Chatterer could n't see him .
Peter sit down and begin to pull his whisker in a way he have when he be try to decide something .
It seem a if two little voice be quarrel inside him .
`` Go along home like the good fellow you be and mind your own business , '' say one .
`` Steal back to the old wall and watch Chatterer and so find out just where his new house be ; he 'll never know anything about it , and there 'll be no harm do , '' say the other little voice .
It be louder than the first voice , and Peter like the sound of it .
`` I believe I will , '' say he , and without wait to hear what the first little voice would say to that , he turn about and very carefully and softly tiptoe back to the old stone wall .
Right near it be a thick little bush .
It seem to Peter that it must have grow there just to give him a hiding place .
He crawl under it and lay very flat .
He could see along the old stone wall in both direction .
Chatterer be sit just where he have leave him .
He be look in the direction that Peter have go when he have say good-by .
Peter chuckle to himself .
`` He 's wait to make sure I have go before he go to that new house of his , '' think Peter .
`` This be the time I 'll fool him . ''

`` You 're not do a bit of harm .
Chatterer have no business to try to keep his new house a secret , anyway , '' say the other little voice inside .
And because of his dreadful curiosity , Peter like the sound of that voice best and listen to it , and after a while the first voice grow discourage and stop .
Chatterer sit where he be for what seem to Peter a very long time .
But by and by he give a sudden funny little flirt of his tail and ran along the old wall a little way .
Then with a hasty look around , he disappear in a hole .
A minute later he pop his head out for another look around and then disappear again .
He do this two or three time a if anxious .
Peter chuckle to himself .
`` That 's his new house right there , '' say he to himself , `` and now that I know where it be , I think I 'll hurry along home to the dear Old Briar-patch . ''
He be just get ready to start when Chatterer pop out of his hole and sit up on a big stone .
He be talk out loud , and Peter listen .
Then his long ear begin to burn , for this be what he hear : `` I 'm glad that Peter 's not a spy , For spy be hateful a can be ; It 's dreadful how some people try Affairs of other folk to see . ''
