His ear still burn , and somehow he do n't feel so tickle over the thought that he have discover Chatterer 's secret a he have think he would .
And over in the hole in the old stone wall Chatterer the Red Squirrel be laugh a if there be some great joke .
There be , and the joke be on Peter Rabbit .
You see he have n't discover Chatterer 's new house at all .
VII HOW CHATTERER HAD FOOLED PETER RABBIT Chatterer the Red Squirrel be a scamp himself and not to be trust .
Nobody in the Green Forest or on the Green Meadows trust him .
And people who can not be trust themselves never trust any one else .
Chatterer never do .
He be always suspicious .
So when Peter Rabbit have say good-by and start for the dear Old Briar-patch without know where Chatterer 's new house be , Chatterer have make up his mind right away that Peter would never be satisfy until he know , or think he know , where that new house be .
You see , he know all about Peter 's dreadful curiosity .
He watch Peter out of sight , then he slip down out of sight himself between the stone of the old wall .
`` I know what Peter will do , '' say he to himself .
`` Peter will come sneak back , and hide where he can watch me , and so find out where my new house be .
I 'll just stay here long enough to give him a chance to hide , and then I 'll fool him . ''
You see , Chatterer know that if he have be in Peter 's place , he would have do just that thing .
So he wait a little while and then go back to the place where Peter have leave him .
There he sit and pretend to be look in the direction in which Peter have go , a if to make sure that Peter be really on his way home .
But all the time Chatterer be watch out of the corner of his eye to see if Peter be hide anywhere near .
He do n't see Peter , but he do n't have the least doubt that Peter be somewhere about .
After a while , he run over to a hole between the stone of the old wall and pretend to be very busy there , just a if it really be the new house he have find .
He keep pop in and out and look around a if afraid that some one be watch him .
He even get some dry leaf and take them inside , a if to make a bed .
All the time , although he have n't see a sign of Peter , he do n't have the least doubt in the world that Peter be watch him .
When he grow tired , a new idea pop into his shrewd little head .
He pop out of the hole and sit up on the wall .
Then he say aloud that verse which have make Peter 's ear burn so .
He have mean to make Peter 's ear burn .
He say that verse just a if he really do believe that Peter be not spy on him and be glad of it .
When he have finish , he whisk out of sight again to give Peter a chance to get away .
But this time Chatterer do some peeking himself .
He hide where Peter could n't see him , but where he himself could see both way along the old stone wall , and so it be that he saw Peter crawl out from under the little bush where he have be hide and sneak away in the direction of the Old Briar-patch .
And he know that this time Peter have go for good .
Then Chatterer laugh and laugh to think how he have fool Peter Rabbit , and wish that he could pat himself on the back for be so smart .
He do n't once think of how dishonest and mean it be of Peter to spy on him , because , you see , he would have do the same thing himself .
`` One have to have one 's wit very sharp these day to keep a secret , '' chuckle Chatterer .
But over in the old Briar-patch that afternoon Peter Rabbit sit very thoughtful and very much ashamed .
The thought that he have find out where Chatterer 's new house be do n't give him the pleasure that he have think it would .
His ear still burn , for he think that Chatterer suppose him honest when he be n't .
`` I believe I 'll go over to-morrow and tell Chatterer all about it and how mean I have be , '' say he at last .
And when he have make up his mind to do this , he felt well .
And all the time he have n't find Chatterer 's new house at all .
You see , it be the old home of Drummer the Woodpecker in an old apple-tree which Chatterer have decide to live in .
VIII CHATTERER GROWS CARELESS When you grow careless even though It be in matter small , Old Mr. Trouble you will find Is bind to make a call .
Some people never seem to learn that .
You would suppose that after all the trouble and worry Chatterer the Red Squirrel have have , he would have learn a lesson .
For a while it seem a if he have .
Morning after morning , before anybody be up in Farmer Brown 's house , he visit Farmer Brown 's corn-crib , take the great care not to be see and to get back to his home in the Old Orchard before it be time for Farmer Brown 's boy to come out and do his morning 's work .
And in the corn-crib he take the great care to steal only where what he take would not be miss .
The empty cob from which he have eat the corn he hide in the darkest corner behind the great pile of yellow corn , where they would not be find until nearly all the corn have be take from the crib .
Oh , he be very sly and crafty , be Chatterer the Red Squirrel -- at first .
But after a while , when nothing happen , Chatterer grow careless .
At first it have seem very dangerous to go over to the corn-crib , but after he have be there often , it do n't seem dangerous at all .
Once inside , he would just give himself up to have a good time .
He race about over the great pile of beautiful yellow corn and find the lovely hiding place in it .
Down in a dark corner he make a splendid bed from piece of husk which have n't be strip from some of the ear .
It be quite the nice place he have ever dream of , be Farmer Brown 's corn-crib .
He get to feel that it be his own and not Farmer Brown 's at all .
The more that feeling grow , the more careless Chatterer become .
He drop a grain of corn now and then and be too lazy to go down and pick it up , or else do n't think anything about it .
Farmer Brown 's boy , come every morning for corn for the hen , notice these grain , but suppose they be some that have be rub from the ear during the handling of them .
Then one morning Chatterer drop a cob from which he have eat all the corn .
He mean to get it and hide it , a he have hide other cob , but he do n't want to do it just then .
And later -- well , then he forget all about it .
Yes , Sir , he forget all about it until he have reach his home in the Old Orchard .
`` Oh , well , '' think Chatterer , `` it do n't matter .
I can get it and hide it to-morrow morning . ''
Now a corn-cob be a very simple thing .
Farmer Brown 's boy know where there be a whole pile of them .
He add to that pile every day , after shell enough corn for the biddy .
So it would seem that there be nothing about a corn-cob to make him open his eye a he do that morning , when he saw the one leave by Chatterer the Red Squirrel .
But you see he know that a bare corn-cob have no business inside the corn-crib , and suddenly those scattered grain of corn have a new meaning for him .
`` Ha , ha ! ''
he exclaim , `` A thief have be here , after all !
I think we be safe from rat and mouse , and I do n't see now how they get in , for I do n't , I really do n't , see how they could climb the stone leg of the corn-crib .
But some one with sharp teeth certainly have be in here .
It must be that I have leave the door open some time , and a rat have slip in .
I 'll just have to get after you , Mr. Rat or Mr . Mouse .
We ca n't have you in our corn-crib . ''
With that he go into the house .
Presently he come back , and in one hand be a rat-trap and in the other a mouse-trap .
IX CHATTERER GROWS TOO CURIOUS Everybody know how curious Peter Rabbit be .
He be forever poke his wobbly little nose in where it have no business to be , and a a result Peter be forever get into trouble .
Whenever Chatterer the Red Squirrel have hear a new story about Peter and the scrape his curiosity have get him into , Chatterer have say that Peter get no more than he deserve .
As for himself , he might be curious about a thing he saw for the first time , but he have too much sense to meddle with it until he know all about it .
So Chatterer have come to be think very smart , quite too smart to be catch in a trap -- at least to be catch in an ordinary trap .
Now a great many people manage to make their neighbor think they be a great deal smart than they really be , and Chatterer be one of this kind .
If some of his neighbor could have peep into Farmer Brown 's corn-crib the morning after Farmer Brown 's boy find the telltale corn-cob so carelessly drop by Chatterer , they would have be surprise .
Yes , Sir , they would have be surprise .
They would have see Chatterer the Red Squirrel , the boaster , he of the sharp wit , show quite as much curiosity a ever possess Peter Rabbit .
Chatterer have come over to the corn-crib a usual to get his daily supply of corn .
As usual , he have race about over the great pile of yellow corn .
Quite suddenly his sharp eye spy something that they have n't see before .
It be down on the floor of the corn-crib quite near the door .
Chatterer be sure that it have n't be there the day before .
It be a very queer look thing , very queer indeed .
And then he spy another queer look thing near it , only this be very much small .
What could they be ?
He look at them suspiciously .
They look harmless enough .
They do n't move .
He run a few step towards them and scold , just a he scold at anything new he find out of door .
Still they do n't move .
He run around on a little ledge where he could look right down on the queer thing .
He be sure now that they be not alive .
The big one he could see all through .
Inside be something to eat .
The little thing be round and flat with funny bit of wire on top .
It look a if it be make of wood , and in the side be little round hole too small for him to put his head through .
`` Leave them alone , '' say a small voice inside of Chatterer .
`` But I want to see what they be and find out all about them , '' say Chatterer .
`` No good ever come of meddle with thing you do n't know about , '' say the small voice .
`` But they be such queer look thing , and they 're not alive .
They ca n't hurt me , '' say Chatterer .
Nevertheless he run back to the pile of corn and try to eat .
Somehow he have lose his appetite .
He could n't take his eye off those two queer thing down on the floor .
`` Better keep away , '' warn the small voice inside .
`` It wo n't do any harm to have a close look at them , '' say Chatterer .
So once more he scramble down from the pile of corn and little by little drew nearer to the two queer thing .
The nearer he get , the more harmless they look .
Finally he reach out and smell of the small .
Then he turn up his nose .
`` Smells of mouse , '' mutter Chatterer , `` just common barn mouse . ''
Then he reach out a paw and touch it .
`` Pooh ! ''
say he , `` it 's nothing to be afraid of . ''
Just then he touch one of the little wire , and there be a sudden snap .
It frighten Chatterer so that he scurry away .
But he could n't stay away .
That snap be such a funny thing , and it have n't do any harm .
You see , he have n't put his paw in at one of the little hole , or it might have do some harm .
Pretty soon he be back again , meddle with those little wire on top .
Every once in a while there would be a snap , and he would scamper away .
It be very scary and great fun .
By and by the thing would n't snap any more , and then Chatterer grow tire of his queer plaything and begin to wonder about the other queer thing .
No harm have come from the first one , and so he be sure no harm could come from the other .
X OLD MR. TROUBLE GETS CHATTERER AT LAST Of course you have guess what it be that Chatterer have be meddle with .
It be a mouse-trap , and he have sprung it without get hurt .
Chatterer do n't know that it be a trap .
He ought to have know , but he do n't .
You see , it be not at all like the trap Farmer Brown 's boy have sometimes set for him in the Green Forest .
He know all about those trap and never , never go near them .
Now that there be nothing more exciting about the mouse-trap , Chatterer turn his attention to the other queer thing .
He walk all around it and look at it from every side .
It certainly be queer .
Yes , Sir , it certainly be queer !
It look something like a little house only he could see all through it .
He put one paw out and touch it .
Nothing happen .
He try it again .
Then he jump right on top of it .
Still nothing happen .
He try his sharp teeth on it , but he could n't bite it .
You see , it be make of stout wire .
Inside be something that look good to eat .
It smell good , too .
Chatterer begin to wonder what it would taste like .
The more he wonder , the more he want to know .
There must be some way of get in , and if he could get in , of course he could get out again .
He jump down to the floor and run all around the queer little wire house .
At each end be a sort of little wire hallway .
Chatterer stick his head in one .
It seem perfectly safe .
He creep a little way in and then back out in a hurry .
Nothing happen .
He try it again .
Still nothing happen .
`` Better keep away , '' say a small voice down inside of him .
`` Pooh !
Who 's afraid ! ''
say Chatterer .
`` This thing ca n't hurt me . ''
Then he creep a little farther in .
Right in front of him be a little round doorway with a little wire door .
Chatterer push the little door with his nose , and it open a teeny , weeny bit .
He draw back suspiciously .
Then he try it again , and this time push the little door a little farther open .
He do this two or three time until finally he have his head quite inside , and there , right down below him , be that food he so want to taste .
`` I can hop right down and get it and then hop right up again , '' think Chatterer .
`` Do n't do it , '' say the small voice inside .
`` Corn be plenty good enough .
Besides , it be time you be get back to the Old Orchard . ''
`` It wo n't take but a minute , '' say Chatterer , `` and I really must know what that taste like . ''
With that he jump down .
Snap !
Chatterer look up .
The little wire door have close .
Old Mr. Trouble have get Chatterer at last .
Yes , Sir , he certainly have get Chatterer this time .
You see , he could n't open that little wire door from the inside .
He be in a trap -- the wire rat-trap set by Farmer Brown 's boy .
XI WHAT HAPPENED NEXT TO CHATTERER Were you ever terribly , terribly frighten ?
That be the way Chatterer felt .
He be catch ; there be no doubt about it !
His sharp teeth be of no use at all on those hard wire .
He could look out between them , but he could n't get out .
He be too frightened to think .
His heart pound against his side until it hurt .
He forget all about that queer food he have so want to taste , and which be right before him now .
Indeed , he felt a if he never , never would want to eat again .
What be go to happen to him now ?
What would Farmer Brown 's boy do to him when he find him there ?
Hark !
What be that ?
It be a step just outside the door of the corn-crib .
Farmer Brown 's boy be come !
Chatterer race around his little wire prison and bit savagely at the hard wire .
But it be of no use , no use at all .
It only hurt his mouth cruelly .
Then the door of the corn-crib swung open , a flood of light pour in , and with it come Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` Hello ! ''
exclaim Farmer Brown 's boy , a he catch sight of Chatterer .
`` So you be the thief who have be steal our corn , and I think it be a rat or a mouse .
Well , well , you little red rascal , do n't you know that thieve come to no good end ?
You 're pretty smart , for I never once think of you , but you be not so smart a you think .
Now I wonder what we have well do with you . ''
He pick up the trap with Chatterer in it and step out into the beautiful great out-of-doors .
Chatterer could see across the dooryard to the Old Orchard and the familiar old stone wall along which he have scamper so often .
They look just the same a ever , and yet -- well , they do n't look just the same , for he could n't look at them without see those cruel wire which be keep him from them .
Farmer Brown 's boy put the trap down on the ground and then begin to call .
`` Puss , Puss , Puss , '' call Farmer Brown 's boy .
Chatterer 's heart , which have be thump so , almost stop beat with fright .
There be Black Pussy , whom he have so often teased and make fun of .
Her yellow eye have a hungry gleam a she walk around the trap and sniffed and sniffed .
Never have Chatterer hear such a terrible sound a those hungry sniff so close to him !
Black Pussy try to put a paw between the wire , and Chatterer saw the great , cruel claw .
But Black Pussy could n't get her paw between the wire .
`` How would you like him for breakfast ? ''
ask Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` Meow , '' say Black Pussy , arch her back and rubbing against his leg .
`` I suppose that mean that you would like him very much , '' laugh Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` Do you think you can catch him if I let him out ? ''
`` Meow , '' reply Black Pussy again , and to poor Chatterer it seem the awfullest sound he ever have hear .
`` Well , we 'll see about it by and by , '' say Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` There 's the breakfast bell , and I have n't feed the biddy yet . ''
XII CHATTERER IS SURE THAT THIS IS HIS LAST DAY There be no hope , not the teeny , weeny ray of hope in the heart of Chatterer , a Farmer Brown 's boy pick up the wire rat-trap and start for the house , Black Pussy , the cat , follow at his heel and look up at Chatterer with cruel , hungry eye .
Chatterer take a farewell look at the Old Orchard and way beyond it the Green Forest , from which he have be drive by fear of Shadow the Weasel .
Then the door of the farmhouse close and shut it all out .
If there have be any hope in Chatterer 's heart , the closing of that door would have shut the last bit out .
But there be n't any hope .
Chatterer be sure that he be to be give to Black Pussy for her breakfast .
Farmer Brown 's boy put the trap on a table .
`` What have you there ? ''
call a great voice .
It be the voice of Farmer Brown himself , who be eat his breakfast .
`` I 've get the thief who have be steal our corn in the crib , '' reply Farmer Brown 's boy , `` and who do you think it be ? ''
`` One of those pesky rat , '' reply Farmer Brown .
`` I 'm afraid you 've be careless and leave the door open some time , and that be how the rat have get in there . ''
`` But it be n't a rat , and I do n't believe that there be a rat there , '' reply Farmer Brown 's boy in triumph .
`` It 's that little scamp of a red squirrel we 've see race along the wall at the edge of the Old Orchard lately .
I ca n't imagine how he get in there , but there he be , and now here he be . ''
`` What be you go to do with him ? ''
ask Farmer Brown , come over to look at Chatterer .
`` I do n't know , '' reply Farmer Brown 's boy , `` unless I give him to Black Puss for her breakfast .
She have be tease me for him ever since I find him . ''
Farmer Brown 's boy look over to the other side of the table a he say this , and his eye twinkle with mischief .
`` Oh , you must n't do that !
That would be cruel ! ''
cry a soft voice .
`` You must take him down to the Green Forest and let him go . ''
A gentle face with pity eye be bent above the trap .
`` Just see how frighten the poor little thing be !
You must take him straight down to the Green Forest right after breakfast . ''
`` Is n't that just like Mother ? ''
cry Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` I believe it would be just the same with the ugly old rat that ever live .
She would try to think of some excuse for let it go . ''
`` God make all the little people who wear fur , and they must have some place in his great plan , '' say Mrs. Brown .
Farmer Brown laugh a big , hearty laugh .
`` True enough , Mother ! ''
say he .
`` The trouble be , they get out of place .
Now this little rascal 's place be down in the Green Forest and not up in our corn-crib . ''
`` Then put him back in his right place ! ''
be the prompt reply , and they all laugh .
Now all this time poor Chatterer be think that this surely be his last day .
You see , he know that he have be a thief , and he know that Farmer Brown 's boy know it .
He just crouch down in a little ball , too miserable to do anything but tremble every time any one come near .
He be sure that he have see for the last time the Green Forest and the Green Meadows and jolly Mr. Sun and all the other beautiful thing he love so , and it seem a if his heart would burst with despair .
XIII CHATTERER IS PUT IN PRISON Who ever do a deed that 's wrong Will surely find some day That for that naughty act of his He 'll surely have to pay .
That be the way with Chatterer .
Of course he have have no business to steal corn from Farmer Brown 's corn-crib .
To be sure he have felt that he have just as much right to that corn a Farmer Brown have .
You see , the little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest feel that everything that grow belongs to them , if they want it and be smart enough to get it before some one else do .
But it be just there that Chatterer go wrong .
Farmer Brown have harvest that corn and store it in his corn-crib , and so , of course , no one else have any right to it .
Right down deep in his heart Chatterer know this .
If he have n't know it , he would n't have be so sly in take what he want .
He know all the time that he be steal , but he try to make himself believe that it be all right .
So he have keep on steal and steal until at last he be catch in a trap , and now he have get to pay for his wrong-doing .
Chatterer be very miserable , so miserable and frighten that he could do nothing but sit huddle up in a little shivery ball .
He have n't the least doubt in the world that this be his very last day , and that Farmer Brown 's boy would turn him over to cruel Black Pussy for her breakfast .
Farmer Brown 's boy have leave him in the trap in the house and have go out .
For a long time Chatterer could hear pound out in the woodshed , and Farmer Brown 's boy be whistle a he pound .
Chatterer wonder how he could whistle and seem so happy when he mean to do such a dreadful thing a to give him to Black Pussy .
After what seem a very long time , age and age , Farmer Brown 's boy come back .
He have with him a queer look box .
`` There , '' say he , `` be a new home for you , you little red imp !
I guess it will keep you out of trouble for a while . ''
He slide back a little door in the top of the box , and then , put on a stout glove and open a little door in the trap , he put in his big hand and close it around Chatterer .
Poor little Chatterer !
He be sure now that this be the end , and that he be to be give to Black Pussy , who be look on with hungry , yellow eye .
He struggle and do his best to bite , but the thick glove give his sharp little teeth no chance to hurt the hand that hold him .
Even in his terror , he notice that that big hand try to be gentle and squeeze him no tight than be necessary .
Then he be lift out of the trap and drop through the little doorway in the top of the queer box , and the door be fasten .
Nothing terrible have happen , after all .
At first , Chatterer just sulk in one corner .
He still felt sure that something terrible be go to happen .
Farmer Brown 's boy take the box out into the shed and put it where the sun shone into it .
For a little while he stay watching , but Chatterer still sulk and sulk .
By and by he go away , take Black Pussy with him , and Chatterer be alone .
When he be quite sure that no one be about , Chatterer begin to wonder what sort of a place he be in , and if there be n't some way to get out .
He find that one side and the top be of fine , stout wire , through which he could look out , and that the other side and the bottom be of wood cover with wire , so that there be no chance for his sharp teeth to gnaw a way out .
In one corner be a stout piece of an apple-tree , with two little stubby branch to sit on , and half way up a little round hole .
Very cautiously Chatterer peep inside the hole .
Inside be a splendid hollow .
On the floor of the box be a little heap of shaving and bit of rag .
And there be a little pile of yellow corn .
How Chatterer do hate the sight of that corn !
You see , it be corn that have get him into all this trouble .
At least , that be the way Chatterer felt about it .
When he have examine everything , he know that there be no way out .
Chatterer be in a prison , though that be not what Farmer Brown 's boy call it .
He say it be a cage .
Illustration : Very cautiously Chatterer peep inside the hole .
XIV CHATTERER DECIDES TO LIVE At first Chatterer decide that he have rather die than live in a prison , no matter how nice that prison might be .
It be a very foolish thing to do , but he make up his mind that he just would n't eat .
He would n't touch that nice , yellow corn Farmer Brown 's boy have put in his prison for him .
He would starve himself to death .
Yes , Sir , he would starve himself to death .
So when he find that there be no way to get out of his prison , he curl up in the little hollow stump in his prison , where no one could see him , and make up his mind that he would stay there until he die .
Life be n't worth live if he have get to spend all the rest of his day in a prison .
He would n't even make himself comfortable .
There be that little heap of nice shaving and bit of rag for him to make a nice comfortable bed of , but he do n't touch them .
No , Sir , he just try to make himself miserable .
Not once that long day do he poke so much a the tip of his nose out of his little round doorway .
Ever so many time Farmer Brown 's boy come to see him , and whistle and call softly to him .
But Chatterer do n't make a sound .
At last night come , and the woodshed where his prison be grow dark and darker and very still .
Now it be about this time that Chatterer 's stomach begin to make itself felt .
Chatterer try not to notice it , but his stomach would be notice , and Chatterer could n't help himself .
His stomach be empty , and it keep tell him so .
`` I 'm go to starve to death , '' say Chatterer to himself over and over .
`` I 'm empty , and there be plenty of food to fill me up , if you 'll only stop be silly , '' whisper his stomach .
The more Chatterer try not to think of how good something to eat would taste , the more he do think of it .
It make him restless and uneasy .
He twist and squirm and turn .
At last he decide that he would have one more look to see if he could n't find some way to get out of his prison .
He poke his head out of the little round doorway .
All be still and dark .
He listen , but not a sound could he hear .
Then he softly creep out and hurriedly examine all the inside of his prison once more .
It be of no use !
There be n't a single place where he could use his sharp teeth .
`` There 's that little pile of corn wait for me , '' whisper his stomach .
`` I 'll never touch it ! ''
say Chatterer fiercely .
Just then he hit something with his foot , and it roll .
He pick it up and then put it down again .
It be a nut , a plump hickory nut .
Two or three time he pick it up and put it down , and each time it be hard than before to put it down .
`` I -- I -- I 'd like to taste one more nut before I starve to death , '' mutter Chatterer , and almost without know it , he begin to gnaw the hard shell .
When that nut be finish , he find another ; and when that be go , still another .
Then he just have to taste a grain of corn .
The first thing Chatterer know , the nut and the corn be all go , and his stomach be full .
Somehow he felt ever so much good .
He do n't feel like starve to death now .
`` I -- I believe I 'll wait a bit and see what happen , '' say he to himself , `` and while I 'm wait , I may as well be comfortable . ''
With that he begin to carry the shaving and rag into the hollow stump and soon have a comfortable a bed a ever he have sleep on .
Chatterer have decide to live .
XV FARMER BROWN 'S BOY TRIES TO MAKE FRIENDS Nobody live who 's wholly bad ; Some good you 'll find in every heart .
Your enemy will be your friend .
If only you will do your part .
All his life Chatterer the Red Squirrel have look on Farmer Brown 's boy a his enemy , just a do all the other little people of the Green Meadows , the Green Forest , and the Smiling Pool .
They fear him , and because they fear him , they hat him .
So whenever he come near , they run away .
Now at first , Farmer Brown 's boy use to run after them for just one thing -- because he want to make friend with them , and he could n't see how ever he be go to do it unless he catch them .
After a while , when he find that he could n't catch them by run after them , he make up his mind that they do n't want to be his friend , and so then he begin to hunt them , because he think it be fun to try to outwit them .
Of course , when he begin to do that , they hat him and fear him all the more .
You see , they do n't understand that really he have one of the kind heart in the world ; and he do n't understand that they hat him just because they do n't know him .
So when Chatterer have be catch in the trap in Farmer Brown 's corn-crib , he have n't doubt in the least that Farmer Brown 's boy would give him to Black Pussy or do something equally cruel ; and even when he find that he be only to be keep a prisoner in a very comfortable prison , with plenty to eat and drink , he be n't willing to believe any good of Farmer Brown 's boy .
Indeed , he hat him more than ever , if that be possible .
But Farmer Brown 's boy be very patient .
He come to Chatterer 's prison ever so many time a day and whistle and cluck and talk to Chatterer .
And he bring good thing to eat .
It seem a if he be all the time try to think of some new treat for Chatterer .
He never come without bring something .
At first , Chatterer would hide in his hollow stump as soon a he saw Farmer Brown 's boy coming and would n't so much a peek out until he have go away .
When he be sure that the way be clear , he would come out again , and always he find some delicious fat nut or some other dainty wait for him .
After a little , as soon a he saw Farmer Brown 's boy come , Chatterer would begin to wonder what good thing he have bring this time , and would grow terribly impatient for Farmer Brown 's boy to go away so that he could find out .
By and by it get so that he could n't wait , but would slyly peep out of his little , round doorway to see what have be bring for him .
Then one day Farmer Brown 's boy do n't come at all .
Chatterer try to make himself believe that he be glad .
He tell himself that he hat Farmer Brown 's boy , and he hop that he never , never would see him again .
But all the time he know that it be n't true .
It be the long day since Chatterer have be a prisoner .
Early the next morning , before Chatterer be out of bed , he hear a step in the woodshed , and before he think what he be do , he be out of his hollow stump to see if it really be Farmer Brown 's boy .
It be , and he have three great fat nut which he drop into Chatterer 's cage .
It seem to Chatterer that he just could n't wait for Farmer Brown 's boy to go away .
Finally he dart forward and seize one .
Then he scamper to the shelter of his hollow stump to eat it .
When it be finish , he just have to have another .
Farmer Brown 's boy be still watch , but somehow Chatterer do n't feel so much afraid .
This time he sit up on one of the little branch of the stump and eat it in plain sight .
Farmer Brown 's boy smile , and it be a pleasant smile .
`` I believe we shall be friend , after all , '' say he .
XVI CHATTERER HAS A PLEASANT SURPRISE Chatterer the Red Squirrel , the mischief maker of the Green Forest , have never be more comfortable in his life .
No matter how rough Brother North Wind roar across the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest , pile the snow in great drift , he could n't send so much a one tiny shiver through the little red coat of Chatterer .
And always right at hand be plenty to eat -- corn and nut and other good thing such a Chatterer love .
No , he never have be so comfortable in all his life .
But he be n't happy , not truly happy .
You see , he be in prison , and no matter how nice a prison may be , no one can be truly happy there .
Since he have be a prisoner , Chatterer have learn to think very differently of Farmer Brown 's boy from what he use to think .
In fact , he and Farmer Brown 's boy have become very good friend , for Farmer Brown 's boy be always very gentle , and always bring him something good to eat .
`` He be n't at all like what I have think , '' say Chatterer , `` and if I be free , I would n't be afraid of him at all .
I -- I 'd like to tell some of the other little Green Forest people about him .
If only -- '' Chatterer do n't finish .
Instead a great lump fill his throat .
You see , he be think of the Green Forest and the Old Orchard , and how he use to race through the tree-tops and along the stone wall .
Half the fun in life have be in run and jumping , and now there be n't room in this little prison to stretch his leg .
If only he could run -- run as hard a ever he know how -- once in a while , he felt that his prison would n't be quite so hard to put up with .
That very afternoon , while Chatterer be take a nap in his bed in the hollow stump , something be slip over his little round doorway , and Chatterer awake in a terrible fright to find himself a prisoner inside his hollow stump .
There be nothing he could do about it but just lie there in his bed , and shake with fright , and wonder what dreadful thing be go to happen next .
He could hear Farmer Brown 's boy very busy about something in his cage .
After a long , long time , his little round doorway let in the light once more .
The door have be open .
At first Chatterer do n't dare go out , but he hear the soft little whistle with which Farmer Brown 's boy always call him when he have something especially nice for him to eat , so at last he peep out .
There on the floor of the cage be some of the nice nut .
Chatterer come out at once .
Then his sharp eye discover something else .
It be a queer look thing make of wire at one end of his cage .
Chatterer look at it with great suspicion .
Could it be a new kind of trap ?
But what would a trap be do there , when he be already a prisoner ?
He eat all the nut , all the time watch this new , queer look thing .
It seem harmless enough .
He go a little nearer .
Finally he hop into it .
It move .
Of course that frighten him , and he start to run up .
But he do n't go up .
No , Sir , he do n't go up .
You see , he be in a wire wheel ; and a he run , the wheel go around .
Chatterer be terribly frighten , and the faster he try to run , the fast the wheel go around .
Finally he have to stop , because he be out of breath and too tired to run another step .
When he stop , the wheel stop .
Little by little , Chatterer begin to understand .
Farmer Brown 's boy have make that wheel to give him a chance to run all he want to and whenever he want to .
When he understand this , Chatterer be a nearly happy a he could be in a prison .
It be such a pleasant surprise !
He would race and race in it until he just have to stop for breath .
Farmer Brown 's boy look on and laugh to see how much happier he have make Chatterer .
XVII SAMMY JAY 'S SHARP EYES Everybody know that Sammy Jay have sharp eye .
In fact , there be very few of the little forest people whose eye be as sharp a Sammy 's .
That be because he use them so much .
A long time ago he find out that the more he use his eye , the sharper they become , and so there be very few minute when Sammy be awake that he be n't try to see something .
He be always look .
That be the reason he always know so much about what be go on in the Green Forest and on the Green Meadows .
Now of course Chatterer the Red Squirrel could n't disappear without be miss , particularly by Sammy Jay .
And of course Sammy could n't miss Chatterer and not wonder what have become of him .

CHAPTER I Danny Meadow Mouse Is Worried Danny Meadow Mouse sit on his door-step with his chin in his hand , and it be very plain to see that Danny have something on his mind .
He have only a nod for Jimmy Skunk , and even Peter Rabbit could get no more than a grumpy `` Good morning . ''
It be n't that he have be catch nap the day before by Reddy Fox and nearly make an end of .
No , it be n't that .
Danny have learn his lesson , and Reddy would never catch him again .
It be n't that he be all alone with no one to play with .
Danny be rather glad that he be alone .
The fact be , Danny Meadow Mouse be worry .
Now worry be one of the bad thing in the world , and it do n't seem a if there be anything that Danny Meadow Mouse need worry about .
But you know it be the easy thing in the world to find something to worry over and make yourself uncomfortable about .
And when you make yourself uncomfortable , you be almost sure to make everyone around you equally uncomfortable .
It be so with Danny Meadow Mouse .
Striped Chipmunk have twice call him `` Cross Patch '' that morning , and Johnny Chuck , who have fight Reddy Fox for him the day before , have call him `` Grumpy . ''
And what do you think be the matter with Danny Meadow Mouse ?
Why , he be worry because his tail be short .
Yes , sir , that be all that ail Danny Meadow Mouse that bright morning .
You know some people let their look make them miserable .
They worry because they be homely or freckle , or short or tall , or thin or stout , all of which be very foolish .
And Danny Meadow Mouse be just a foolish in worry because his tail be short .
It be short !
It certainly be all of that !
Danny never have realize how short until he chance to meet his cousin Whitefoot , who live in the Green Forest .
He be very elegantly dress , but the most imposing thing about him be his long , slim , beautiful tail .
Danny have at once become conscious of his own stubby little tail , and he have hardly have pride enough to hold his head up a become an honest Meadow Mouse .
Ever since he have be think and thinking , and wonder how his family come to have such short tail .
Then he grow envious and begin to wish and wish and wish that he could have a long tail like his cousin Whitefoot .
He be so busy wish that he have a long tail that he quite forget to take care of the tail he do have , and he pretty nearly lose it and his life with it .
Old Whitetail the Marsh Hawk spy Danny sit there mop on his doorstep , and come sailing over the top of the meadow grass so softly that he all but catch Danny .
If it have n't be for one of the Merry Little Breezes , Danny would have be catch .
And all because he be envious .
It 's a bad , bad habit .
CHAPTER II Danny Meadow Mouse and His Short Tail All Danny Meadow Mouse could think about be his short tail .

Pretty soon his friend begin to pass without stop .

`` What 's the matter ? ''
ask old Mr. Toad .
`` Nothing , '' reply Danny Meadow Mouse .
`` I do n't suppose there really be anything the matter , but what do you think be the matter ? ''
say old Mr. Toad .
Danny fidget , and old Mr. Toad look up at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun and wink .
`` Sun be just as bright a ever , be n't it ? ''
he inquire .
`` Yes , '' say Danny .
`` Got plenty to eat and drink , have n't you ? ''
continued Mr. Toad .
`` Yes , '' say Danny .
`` Seems to me that that be a pretty good-looking suit of clothes you 're wear , '' say Mr. Toad , eye Danny critically .
`` Sunny weather , plenty to eat and drink , and good clothes -- must be you do n't know when you 're well off , Danny Meadow Mouse . ''
Danny hang his head .
Finally he look up and catch a kindly twinkle in old Mr. Toad 's eye .
`` Mr. Toad , how can I get a long tail like my cousin Whitefoot of the Green Forest ? ''
he ask .
`` So that 's what 's the matter !
Ha !
ha !
ha !
Danny Meadow Mouse , I 'm ashamed of you !
I certainly be ashamed of you ! ''
say Mr. Toad .
`` What good would a long tail do you ?
Tell me that . ''
For a minute Danny do n't know just what to say .
`` I -- I -- I 'd look so much good if I have a long tail , '' he venture .
Old Mr. Toad just laugh .
`` You never saw a Meadow Mouse with a long tail , do you ?
Of course not .
What a sight it would be !
Why , everybody on the Green Meadows would laugh themselves sick at the sight !
You see you need to be slim and trim and handsome to carry a long tail well .
And then what a nuisance it would be !
You would always have to be think of your tail and take care to keep it out of harm 's way .
Look at me .
I 'm homely .
Some folk call me ugly to look at .
But no one try to catch me a Farmer Brown 's boy do Billy Mink because of his fine coat ; and no one want to put me in a cage because of a fine voice .
I be satisfied to be just a I be , and if you 'll take my advice , Danny Meadow Mouse , you 'll be satisfy to be just a you be . ''

`` Perhaps you be right , '' say Danny Meadow Mouse after a little .
`` I 'll try . ''
CHAPTER III Danny Meadow Mouse Plays Hide and Seek Life be always a game of hide and seek to Danny Meadow Mouse .
You see , he be such a fat little fellow that there be a great many other furry-coated people , and almost a many who wear feather , who would gobble Danny up for breakfast or for dinner if they could .
Some of them pretend to be his friend , but Danny always keep his eye open when they be around and always begin to play hide and seek .
Peter Rabbit and Jimmy Skunk and Striped Chipmunk and Happy Jack Squirrel be all friend whom he can trust , but he always have a bright twinkle eye open for Reddy Fox and Billy Mink and Shadow the Weasel and old Whitetail the Marsh Hawk , and several more , especially Hooty the Owl at night .
Now Danny Meadow Mouse be a stout-hearted little fellow , and when rough Brother North Wind come shout across the Green Meadows , tear to piece the snow cloud and shake out the snowflake until they cover the Green Meadows deep , deep , deep , Danny just snuggle down in his warm coat in his snug little house of grass and wait .
Danny like the snow .
Yes , sir , Danny Meadow Mouse like the snow .
He just love to dig in it and make tunnel .
Through those tunnel in every direction he could go where he please and when he please without be see by anybody .
It be great fun !
Every little way he make a little round doorway up beside a stiff stalk of grass .
Out of this he could peep at the white world , and he could get the fresh cold air .
Sometimes , when he be quite sure that no one be around , he would scamper across on top of the snow from one doorway to another , and when he do this , he make the pretty little footprint .
Now Reddy Fox know all about those doorway and who make them .
Reddy be have hard work to get enough to eat this cold weather , and he be hungry most of the time .
One morning , a he come tiptoe softly over the meadow , what should he see just ahead of him but the head of Danny Meadow Mouse pop out of one of those little round doorway .
Reddy 's mouth water , and he steal forward more softly than ever .
When he get within jump distance , he draw his stout hind legs under him and make ready to spring .
Presto !
Danny Meadow Mouse have disappear !
Reddy Fox jump just the same and begin to dig as fast a he could make his paw go .
He could smell Danny Meadow Mouse and that make him almost frantic .
All the time Danny Meadow Mouse be scurry along one of his little tunnel , and when finally Reddy Fox stop dig because he be quite out of breath , Danny pop his head out of another little doorway and laugh at Reddy .
Of course Reddy saw him , and of course Reddy try to catch him there , and dig frantically just a before .
And of course Danny Meadow Mouse be n't there .
After a while Reddy Fox grow tire of this kind of a game and try another plan .
The next time he saw Danny Meadow Mouse stick his head out , Reddy pretend not to see him .
He stretch himself out on the ground and make believe that he be very tired and sleepy .
He close his eye .
Then he open them just the tiny bit , so that he could see Danny Meadow Mouse and yet seem to be asleep .
Danny watch him for a long time .
Then he chuckle to himself and drop out of sight .
No sooner be he go than Reddy Fox stole over close to the little doorway and wait .
`` He 'll surely stick his head out again to see if I 'm asleep , and then I 'll have him , '' say Reddy to himself .
So he wait and wait and wait .
By and by he turn his head .
There be Danny Meadow Mouse at another little doorway laugh at him !

CHAPTER IV Old Granny Fox Tries for Danny Meadow Mouse Danny Meadow Mouse have not enjoy anything so much for a long time a he do that game of hide and seek .

But Danny never let himself think about this .
He have enjoy the game all the more because it have be such a dangerous game .
It have be such fun to dive into one of his little round doorways in the snow , run along one of his own little tunnel , and then peep out at another doorway and watch Reddy Fox dig as fast a ever he could at the doorway Danny have just leave .

Granny listen with her head cock on one side .

Danny have felt in his bone that Reddy would come back , so he be watch , and he saw them as soon a they come out of the Green Forest .

Suddenly something plunge down through the snow right at his very heel .
Danny do n't have to look to know that it be Granny Fox herself , and he squeak with fright .
CHAPTER V What Happened on the Green Meadows Thick and fast thing be happen to Danny Meadow Mouse down on the snow-covered Green Meadows .

CHAPTER VI Danny Meadow Mouse Remembers and Reddy Fox Forgets `` There he go ! ''

CHAPTER VIII Brother North Wind Proves a Friend Danny Meadow Mouse have see nothing of old Granny Fox or Reddy Fox for several day .

CHAPTER IX Danny Meadow Mouse Is Caught at Last `` Tippy-toppy-tippy-toe , Play and frolic in the snow !

CHAPTER X A Strange Ride and How It Ended Danny Meadow Mouse often have sit watch Skimmer the Swallow sailing around up in the blue , blue sky .

He be be carry .

he land in the soft snow right in the very middle of the Old Briar-patch , and the last thing he remember be hear the scream of disappointment and rage of Hooty the Owl .
CHAPTER XI Peter Rabbit Gets a Fright Peter Rabbit sit in his favorite place in the middle of the dear Old Briar-patch , try to decide which way he would go on his travel that night .
The night before he have have a narrow escape from old Granny Fox over in the Green Forest .
There be nothing to eat around the Smiling Pool and no one to talk to there any more , and you know that Peter must either eat or ask question in order to be perfectly happy .
No , the Smiling Pool be too dull a place to interest Peter on such a beautiful moonlight night , and Peter have no mind to try his leg against those of old Granny Fox again in the Green Forest .
Early that morning , just after Peter have settle down for his morning nap , Tommy Tit the Chickadee have drop into the dear Old Briar-patch just to be neighborly .
Peter be just doze off when he hear the cheery little voice in the world .
It be say : `` Dee-dee-chickadee !
I see you !
Can you see me ? ''
Peter begin to smile even before he could get his eye open and look up .
There , right over his head , be Tommy Tit hang head down from a nod old bramble .
In a twinkling he be down on the snow right in front of Peter , then up in the bramble again , right side up , upside down , here , there , everywhere , never still a minute , and all the time chatter away in the cheery little voice in the world .
`` Dee-dee-chickadee !
I 'm as happy a can be !
Find it much the good way To be happy all the day .
Dee-dee-chickadee !
Everybody 's good to me ! ''
`` Hello , Tommy ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` Where 'd you come from ? ''
`` From Farmer Brown 's new orchard up on the hill .
It 's a fine orchard , Peter Rabbit , a fine orchard .
I go there every morning for my breakfast .
If the winter last long enough , I 'll have all the tree clean up for Farmer Brown . ''
Peter look puzzle .
`` What do you mean ? ''
he ask .
`` Just what I say , '' reply Tommy Tit , almost turn a somersault in the air .
`` There 's a million egg of insect on those young peach tree , but I 'm clear them all off as fast a I can .
They 're mighty fine eating , Peter Rabbit , mighty fine eating ! ''
And with that Tommy Tit have say good-by and flit away .
Peter be think of that young orchard now , a he sit in the moonlight try to make up his mind where to go .
The thought of those young peach tree make his mouth water .
It be a long way up to the orchard on the hill , a very long way , and Peter be wonder if it really be safe to go .
He have just about make up his mind to try it , for Peter be very , very fond of the bark of young peach tree , when thump !
something drop out of the sky at his very foot .
It startle Peter so that he nearly tumble over backward .
And right at the same instant come the fierce , angry scream of Hooty the Owl .
That almost make Peter 's heart stop beating , although he know that Hooty could n't get him down there in the Old Briar-patch .
When Peter get his wit together and his heart do n't go so jumpy , he look to see what have drop so close to him out of the sky .
His big eye grow big than ever , and he rub them to make quite sure that he really saw what he think he saw .
Yes , there be no doubt about it -- there at his foot lay Danny Meadow Mouse !
-LSB- Illustration : Peter Rabbit be surprise to see Danny . -RSB-
CHAPTER XII The Old Briar-patch Has a New Tenant Danny Meadow Mouse slowly open his eye and then close them again quickly , a if afraid to look around .
He could hear someone talk .
It be a pleasant voice , not at all like the terrible voice of Hooty the Owl , which be the very last thing that Danny Meadow Mouse could remember .
Danny lay still a minute and listen .
`` Why , Danny Meadow Mouse , where in the world do you drop from ? ''
ask the voice .
It sound like -- why , very much like Peter Rabbit speaking .
Danny open his eye again .
It be Peter Rabbit .
`` Where -- where be I ? ''
ask Danny Meadow Mouse in a very weak and small voice .
`` In the middle of the dear Old Briar-patch with me , '' reply Peter Rabbit .
`` But how do you get here ?
You seem to drop right out of the sky . ''
Danny Meadow Mouse shudder .
Suddenly he remember everything : how Hooty the Owl have catch him in great cruel claw and have carry him through the moonlight across the snow-covered Green Meadows ; how he have felt Hooty 's claw slip and then have struggle and kick and twist and turn until his coat have tear and he have drop down , down , down until he have land in the soft snow and knock all the breath out of his little body .
The very last thing he could remember be Hooty 's fierce scream of rage and disappointment .
Danny shudder again .
Then a new thought come to him .
He must get out of sight !
Hooty might catch him again !
Danny try to scramble to his foot .
`` Ouch !
Oh ! ''
groan Danny and lay still again .
`` There , there .
Keep still , Danny Meadow Mouse .
There 's nothing to be afraid of here , '' say Peter Rabbit gently .
His big eye fill with tear a he look at Danny Meadow Mouse , for Danny be all torn and hurt by the cruel claw of Hooty the Owl , and you know Peter have a very tender heart .
So Danny lay still , and while Peter Rabbit try to make him comfortable and dress his hurt , he tell Peter all about how he have forget to watch up in the sky and so have be catch by Hooty the Owl , and all about his terrible ride in Hooty 's cruel claw .
`` Oh , dear , whatever shall I do now ? ''
he end .
`` However shall I get back home to my warm house of grass , my safe little tunnel under the snow , and my little store of seed in the snug hollow in the old fence-post ? ''
Peter Rabbit look thoughtful .
`` You ca n't do it , '' say he .
`` You simply ca n't do it .
It be such a long way for a little fellow like you that it would n't be safe to try .
If you go at night , Hooty the Owl might catch you again .
If you try in daylight , old Roughleg the Hawk would be almost sure to see you .
And night or day old Granny Fox or Reddy Fox might come snoop around , and if they do , they would be sure to catch you .
I tell you what , you stay right here !
The dear Old Briar-patch be the safe place in the world .
Why , just think , here you can come out in broad daylight and laugh at Granny and Reddy Fox and at old Roughleg the Hawk , because the good old bramble will keep them out , if they try to get you .
You can make just as good tunnel under the snow here a you have there , and there be lot and lot of seed on the ground to eat .
You know I do n't care for them myself .
I 'm lonesome sometimes , live here all alone .
You stay here , and we 'll have the Old Briar-patch to ourselves . ''
Danny Meadow Mouse look at Peter gratefully .
`` I will , and thank you ever so much , Peter Rabbit , '' he say .
And this be how the dear Old Briar-patch happen to have another tenant .
CHAPTER XIII Peter Rabbit Visits the Peach Orchard `` Do n't go , Peter Rabbit !
Do n't go ! ''
beg Danny Meadow Mouse .
Peter hop to the edge of the Old Briar-patch and look over the moonlit , snow-covered meadow to the hill back of Farmer Brown 's house .
On that hill be the young peach orchard of which Tommy Tit the Chickadee have tell him , and ever since Peter 's mouth have water and water every time he think of those young peach tree and the tender bark on them .
`` I think I will , Danny , just this once , '' say Peter .
`` It 's a long way , and I 've never be there before ; but I guess it 's just as safe a the Meadows or the Green Forest .
`` Oh I 'm as bold a bold can be !
Sing hoppy-hippy-hippy-hop-o !
I 'll hie me forth the world to see !
Sing hoppy-hippy-hippy-hop-o !
My ear be long , My leg be strong , So now good day ; I 'll hie away !
Sing hoppy-hippy-hippy-hop-o ! ''
And with that , Peter Rabbit leave the dear safe Old Briar-patch , and away he go lipperty-lipperty-lip , across the Green Meadows towards the hill and the young orchard back of Farmer Brown 's house .
Danny Meadow Mouse watch him go and shake his head in disapproval .
`` Foolish , foolish , foolish ! ''
he say over and over to himself .
`` Why ca n't Peter be content with the good thing that he have ? ''
Peter Rabbit hurry along through the moonlight , stop every few minute to sit up to look and listen .
He hear the fierce hunt call of Hooty the Owl way over in the Green Forest , so he felt sure that at present there be nothing to fear from him .
He know that since their return to the Green Meadows and the Green Forest , Granny and Reddy Fox have keep away from Farmer Brown 's , so he do not worry about them .
All in good time Peter come to the young orchard .
It be just a Tommy Tit the Chickadee have tell him .
Peter hop up to the near peach tree and nibble the bark .
